# Volt Documentation

RakNet
======

The **RakNet** library provides low-level access to outgoing game packets.

Interacting with RakNet is unsafe and can lead to account terminations, broken game behavior, disconnects, or other unintended side effects. Do not use this library unless you understand the risks and know exactly what you are doing.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#overview)

------------------------------------------------------

RakNet allows you to:

*   Inspect outgoing packets before they are sent
*   Modify or block packets in a send hook
*   Send custom packet payloads manually
*   Work with packet data as a buffer, string, or byte array

[Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#functions)

--------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `raknet.add_send_hook` | Register a callback that runs before a packet is sent |
| `raknet.remove_send_hook` | Remove a callback registered with `raknet.add_send_hook` |
| `raknet.send` | Send a packet with a payload, priority, reliability, and ordering channel |

[Packet API](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#packet-api)

----------------------------------------------------------

### [Methods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#methods)

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `RakNetPacket:SetData` | Replace the packet payload |
| `RakNetPacket:Block` | Prevent the packet from being sent |

### [Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#properties)

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `RakNetPacket.AsBuffer` | `buffer` | Packet data as a buffer |
| `RakNetPacket.AsString` | `string` | Packet data as a string |
| `RakNetPacket.AsArray` | `{number}` | Packet data as an array of bytes |
| `RakNetPacket.Priority` | `number` | Packet priority |
| `RakNetPacket.Reliability` | `number` | Packet reliability |
| `RakNetPacket.OrderingChannel` | `number` | Packet ordering channel |
| `RakNetPacket.Size` | `number` | Packet payload size in bytes |

[Hook Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#hook-syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    raknet.add_send_hook(hook: (packet: RakNetPacket) -> ()) -> ()
    raknet.remove_send_hook(hook: (packet: RakNetPacket) -> ()) -> ()

[Send Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#send-syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    raknet.send(
        data: buffer | string | {number},
        priority: number,
        reliability: number,
        ordering_channel: number
    ) -> ()

[Packet Method Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#packet-method-syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    RakNetPacket:SetData(data: buffer | string | {number}) -> ()
    RakNetPacket:Block() -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------

### [`raknet.add_send_hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#raknetadd_send_hook)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `hook` | `(packet: RakNetPacket) -> ()` | Callback fired before a packet is sent |

### [`raknet.remove_send_hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#raknetremove_send_hook)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `hook` | `(packet: RakNetPacket) -> ()` | Previously registered send hook |

### [`raknet.send`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#raknetsend)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | \`buffer | string |
| `priority` | `number` | RakNet send priority |
| `reliability` | `number` | RakNet reliability mode |
| `ordering_channel` | `number` | Ordering channel used for ordered traffic |

### [`RakNetPacket:SetData`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#raknetpacketsetdata)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | \`buffer | string |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#returns)

----------------------------------------------------

All `raknet` functions and `RakNetPacket` methods documented here do not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#description)

------------------------------------------------------------

`raknet.add_send_hook` lets you intercept outgoing packets before they are sent. Inside a hook, you can inspect packet metadata, read its payload in multiple formats, replace the payload with `RakNetPacket:SetData`, or stop transmission entirely with `RakNetPacket:Block`.

`raknet.send` sends a custom packet payload using the provided priority, reliability, and ordering channel. Payload data may be supplied as a `buffer`, a `string`, or an array of byte values.

Because this library operates at the packet level, mistakes can be difficult to debug and may have immediate consequences. Keep hooks minimal, validate payloads carefully, and avoid modifying traffic unless absolutely necessary.

[Example: Logging Outgoing Packets](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#example-logging-outgoing-packets)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function packetLogger(packet)
        print("Outgoing packet:")
        print("  Size:", packet.Size)
        print("  Priority:", packet.Priority)
        print("  Reliability:", packet.Reliability)
        print("  Ordering channel:", packet.OrderingChannel)
    end
    
    raknet.add_send_hook(packetLogger)

[Example: Blocking a Packet](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#example-blocking-a-packet)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function blockLargePackets(packet)
        if packet.Size > 512 then
            warn("Blocked packet larger than 512 bytes")
            packet:Block()
        end
    end
    
    raknet.add_send_hook(blockLargePackets)

[Example: Replacing Packet Data](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#example-replacing-packet-data)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function rewritePacket(packet)
        local bytes = packet.AsArray
    
        if #bytes > 0 then
            bytes[1] = 0x01
            packet:SetData(bytes)
        end
    end
    
    raknet.add_send_hook(rewritePacket)

[Example: Sending a Packet](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#example-sending-a-packet)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local payload = { 0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04 }
    
    raknet.send(payload, 0, 0, 0)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#notes)

------------------------------------------------

*   Hooks run before the packet is sent
*   `RakNetPacket:Block()` prevents the current packet from being transmitted
*   `RakNetPacket:SetData()` replaces the packet payload in-place
*   Packet data can be read and written as a `buffer`, `string`, or byte array
*   Invalid payloads or incorrect metadata can disconnect clients or break protocol behavior

[oth.unhook\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook)
[Reflection\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

### On this page

[`raknet.add_send_hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet#raknetadd_send_hook)

Introduction
============

The official documentation for **Volt**

The environment docs are heavily based on the [sUNC](https://sunc.su/)
 (senS' Unified Naming Convention) standard.

Here you can find information about Volt's scripting environment and other general usage information.

This documentation is subject to refactoring and may not remain exactly the same

# Volt Documentation

Cache
=====

The **Cache** library provides functions for manipulating the instance reference cache.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache#overview)

-----------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Replace cached instance references
*   Invalidate cached references
*   Check if an instance is cached

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache#available-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`cache.replace`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace) | Replace a cached instance reference |
| [`cache.invalidate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate) | Remove an instance from the cache |
| [`cache.iscached`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached) | Check if an instance is cached |

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`cloneref`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref) | Clone an instance reference |
| [`compareinstances`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances) | Compare two instance references |

# Volt Documentation

[oth](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)

oth.unhook
==========

Removes a hook created with `oth.hook`.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------

    oth.unhook(target: function) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `target` | `function` | The hooked function to remove |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the hook was successfully removed |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------

`oth.unhook` removes a hook from a function that was created with `oth.hook`. The function is restored to its original behavior.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#example)

--------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook a function
    local originalFunc = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        print("Hooked:", ...)
        return originalFunc(...)
    end)
    
    -- Later, remove the hook
    local success = oth.unhook(someCFunction)
    if success then
        print("Hook removed successfully")
    end

[Check Hook Status](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#check-hook-status)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalFunc = oth.hook(print, function(...)
        print("[HOOKED]", ...)
    end)
    
    -- Remove hook
    if oth.unhook(print) then
        print("Hook removed")
    else
        print("No hook to remove")
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#notes)

----------------------------------------------------

*   Only works on functions hooked with `oth.hook`
*   Returns `false` if the function wasn't hooked or hook removal failed
*   The original function reference from `oth.hook` remains valid after unhooking

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`oth.hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)
     - Create a hook
*   [`oth.get_root_callback`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback)
     - Get original function

[oth.is\_hook\_thread\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread)
[RakNet\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/raknet)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#parameters)

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook#description)

# Volt Documentation

oth
===

The **oth** library provides secure alternatives to `hookfunction` for C functions. Hooks are executed on separate threads, providing better isolation and safety.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#overview)

---------------------------------------------------

The `oth` library allows you to:

*   Hook C functions securely on separate threads
*   Remove hooks when no longer needed
*   Access the original function even after multiple hooks
*   Detect if code is running in a hook thread

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#available-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`oth.hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook) | Hook a C function on a separate thread |
| [`oth.unhook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook) | Remove a hook created with `oth.hook` |
| [`oth.get_root_callback`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback) | Get the original function |
| [`oth.is_hook_thread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread) | Check if running in a hook thread |
| [`get_original_thread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread) | Get the original thread |

[Why Use oth?](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#why-use-oth)

----------------------------------------------------------

Unlike `hookfunction`, `oth.hook` executes hooks on separate threads, providing:

*   **Better isolation** - Hooks don't interfere with the main thread
*   **Improved safety** - Reduces risk of crashes from hook conflicts
*   **Thread awareness** - Know when you're in a hook context

[Related Libraries](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#related-libraries)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`closures`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)
     - Standard function hooking with `hookfunction`

[setfpscap\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap)
[get\_original\_thread\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#available-functions)
[Why Use oth?](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#why-use-oth)
[Related Libraries](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth#related-libraries)

# Volt Documentation

Encoding
========

The **Encoding** library provides functions for encoding and decoding data in various formats.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding#overview)

--------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Convert data to and from Base64
*   Compress and decompress data using LZ4

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding#available-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`base64decode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode) | Decode a Base64 string |
| [`base64encode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode) | Encode data to Base64 |
| [`lz4compress`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress) | Compress data using LZ4 |
| [`lz4decompress`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress) | Decompress LZ4 data |

[setrenderproperty\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode)

# Volt Documentation

Drawing
=======

The **Drawing** library provides functions for creating and managing visual overlays that render on top of the Roblox viewport.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#overview)

-------------------------------------------------------

Drawing objects allow you to create:

*   Lines and shapes
*   Text labels
*   Images
*   Custom UI elements

These drawings are rendered directly on the screen and are not part of the Roblox UI system, making them hidden from game scripts.

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#available-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`cleardrawcache`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache) | Clear all cached drawing objects |
| [`getrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty) | Get a property from a drawing object |
| [`isrenderobj`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj) | Check if a value is a drawing object |
| [`setrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty) | Set a property on a drawing object |

[Creating Drawing Objects](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#creating-drawing-objects)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `Drawing.new(type)` to create new drawing objects:

    local line = Drawing.new("Line")
    line.From = Vector2.new(0, 0)
    line.To = Vector2.new(100, 100)
    line.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    line.Thickness = 2
    line.Visible = true

[Drawing Types](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#drawing-types)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Line` | A line between two points |
| `Circle` | A circle with center and radius |
| `Square` | A rectangle |
| `Triangle` | A triangle with three vertices |
| `Text` | Text label |
| `Image` | An image/texture |
| `Quad` | A quadrilateral with four vertices |

[Common Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#common-properties)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

All drawing objects share these properties:

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Visible` | `boolean` | Whether the object is visible |
| `ZIndex` | `number` | Rendering order (higher = on top) |
| `Transparency` | `number` | Transparency (0 = opaque, 1 = invisible) |
| `Color` | `Color3` | The object's color |

[Cleanup](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#cleanup)

-----------------------------------------------------

Always remove drawing objects when done:

    local circle = Drawing.new("Circle")
    -- ... use the circle ...
    circle:Remove()

[debug.validlevel\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel)
[cleardrawcache\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#available-functions)
[Creating Drawing Objects](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#creating-drawing-objects)
[Drawing Types](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#drawing-types)
[Common Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#common-properties)
[Cleanup](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing#cleanup)

# Volt Documentation

Environment
===========

The **Environment** library provides functions for accessing and manipulating the Lua environment, including garbage collection inspection and global environments.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#overview)

-----------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Access different global environments
*   Inspect the garbage collector
*   Filter and find objects in memory

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#available-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`filtergc`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc) | Filter garbage collected objects |
| [`getgc`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc) | Get all objects tracked by garbage collector |
| [`getgenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv) | Get volt's global environment |
| [`getreg`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg) | Get the Lua registry |
| [`getrenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv) | Get the game's global environment |
| [`gettenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv) | Get a thread's environment |

[Environment Types](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#environment-types)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Volt Environment (genv)](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#volt-environment-genv)

The global environment where your scripts run. Variables defined here persist across script executions.

### [Game Environment (renv)](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#game-environment-renv)

The game's Lua environment containing Roblox globals like `game`, `workspace`, etc.

### [Registry](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment#registry)

The Lua registry is a special table used internally by the Lua implementation to store references.

\

[filtergc\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc)

# Volt Documentation

Actors
======

The **Actors** library provides functions for working with Roblox's parallel Luau actors and Lua state management.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#overview)

------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Get and manage actors in the game
*   Run code on specific actor threads
*   Create communication channels between actors
*   Check parallel execution state
*   Access and control Lua execution states
*   Monitor actor state creation

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#available-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`create_comm_channel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel) | Create a communication channel |
| [`get_comm_channel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel) | Get an existing communication channel |
| [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors) | Get all actors in the game |
| [`getactorstates`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates) | Get all active LuaStateProxy objects |
| [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate) | Get LuaStateProxy for actor or script |
| [`getgamestate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getgamestate) | Get the default game Lua state |
| [`isparallel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel) | Check if running in parallel |
| [`on_actor_added`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added) | Event fired when actor is ready |
| [`on_actor_state_created`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created) | Event fired when actor state is created |
| [`run_on_actor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor) | Execute code on an actor |

[What are Actors?](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#what-are-actors)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

Actors are Roblox's way of enabling parallel Luau execution. They allow scripts to run concurrently on multiple threads, improving performance for computationally intensive tasks.

[Communication Channels](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#communication-channels)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Communication channels allow actors to send messages to each other. Use `create_comm_channel` to create a channel and `get_comm_channel` to retrieve it from another actor.

[Introduction\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs)
[create\_comm\_channel\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#available-functions)
[What are Actors?](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#what-are-actors)
[Communication Channels](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors#communication-channels)

Crypt
=====

The **Crypt** library provides cryptographic functions for encryption, hashing, and random number generation.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt#overview)

-----------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Encrypt and decrypt data
*   Generate cryptographic hashes
*   Create secure random values
*   Perform HMAC authentication

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt#available-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`crypt.encrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt) | Encrypt data with a key |
| [`crypt.decrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt) | Decrypt data with a key |
| [`crypt.hash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash) | Generate a hash of data |
| [`crypt.hmac`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac) | Generate HMAC authentication code |
| [`crypt.random`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random) | Generate random bytes |
| [`crypt.generatekey`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey) | Generate a random encryption key |
| [`crypt.generatebytes`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes) | Generate random bytes |

[Note](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt#note)

---------------------------------------------

Base64 encoding functions (`crypt.base64encode`, `crypt.base64decode`) and LZ4 compression functions (`crypt.lz4compress`, `crypt.lz4decompress`) are documented in the [Encoding](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding)
 section.

# Volt Documentation

Metatable
=========

The **Metatable** library provides functions for working with metatables and metamethods on Roblox objects.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable#overview)

---------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Access raw metatables on locked objects
*   Modify metatable read-only status
*   Get the namecall method in hooks

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable#available-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`getnamecallmethod`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod) | Get the method name in a namecall hook |
| [`getrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable) | Get the raw metatable of an object |
| [`isreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly) | Check if a table is read-only |
| [`iswritable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable) | Check if a table is writable |
| [`makereadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly) | Make a table read-only |
| [`makewritable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable) | Make a table writable |
| [`setnamecallmethod`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod) | Set the method name in a namecall hook |
| [`setrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable) | Set the raw metatable of an object |
| [`setreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly) | Set a table's read-only status |

[Understanding Metatables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable#understanding-metatables)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Metatables in Lua control the behavior of tables and userdata. They define how objects respond to operations like indexing, calling, and arithmetic.

### [Common Metamethods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable#common-metamethods)

| Metamethod | Triggered By |
| --- | --- |
| `__index` | Reading a missing key (`obj.key`) |
| `__newindex` | Writing to a key (`obj.key = value`) |
| `__namecall` | Method calls (`obj:method()`) |
| `__call` | Calling as function (`obj()`) |
| `__tostring` | String conversion (`tostring(obj)`) |

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod)

Scripts
=======

The **Scripts** library provides functions for interacting with running scripts, loading modules, and compiling code.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts#overview)

-------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Get references to running scripts
*   Access script environments
*   Load and compile Lua code
*   Extract script information

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts#available-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`getcallingscript`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript) | Get the script that called the current function |
| [`getloadedmodules`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules) | Get all loaded ModuleScripts |
| [`getmodules`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules) | Get all ModuleScripts in the game |
| [`getrunningscripts`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getrunningscripts) | Get all running scripts |
| [`getscriptbytecode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode) | Get a script's compiled bytecode |
| [`getscriptclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure) | Get a script's main function |
| [`getscriptfromthread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread) | Get the script associated with a thread |
| [`getscripthash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash) | Get a hash of a script's bytecode |

# Volt Documentation

Filesystem
==========

The **Filesystem** library provides functions for reading, writing, and managing files on the local system.

You cannot access files outside the workspace folder for security reasons, unless an explicit symlink is created within the workspace folder.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem#overview)

----------------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   Read and write files
*   Create and delete files and folders
*   Check if files and folders exist
*   List directory contents

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem#available-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`appendfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile) | Append data to a file |
| [`delfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile) | Delete a file |
| [`delfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder) | Delete a folder |
| [`dofile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile) | Load and execute a Lua file |
| [`getcustomasset`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset) | Get a content URL for a local file |
| [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile) | Check if a path is a file |
| [`isfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder) | Check if a path is a folder |
| [`listfiles`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles) | List files in a folder |
| [`loadfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile) | Load a Lua file as a function |
| [`makefolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder) | Create a folder |
| [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile) | Read contents of a file |
| [`writefile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile) | Write data to a file |

[Workspace Folder](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem#workspace-folder)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

All file operations are relative to volt's workspace folder. This is a sandboxed directory that prevents access to sensitive system files.

    -- These are relative to the workspace folder
    writefile("myfile.txt", "Hello")        -- workspace/myfile.txt
    writefile("subfolder/file.txt", "Hi")   -- workspace/subfolder/file.txt

[gettenv\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv)
[appendfile\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem#available-functions)

# Volt Documentation

Debug
=====

The **Debug** library provides functions for runtime inspection of Luau functions, including access to constants, upvalues, protos, and stack values.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#overview)

-----------------------------------------------------

These functions allow you to:

*   **Inspect** function internals (constants, upvalues, protos)
*   **Modify** function behavior at runtime
*   **Access** the call stack

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#available-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`debug.getcallstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack) | Get the current call stack |
| [`debug.getconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant) | Get a constant from a function |
| [`debug.getconstants`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants) | Get all constants from a function |
| [`debug.getinfo`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo) | Get information about a function |
| [`debug.getproto`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto) | Get a proto (nested function) from a function |
| [`debug.getprotos`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos) | Get all protos from a function |
| [`debug.getstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack) | Get a value from the stack |
| [`debug.getupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue) | Get an upvalue from a function |
| [`debug.getupvalues`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues) | Get all upvalues from a function |
| [`debug.setconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant) | Set a constant in a function |
| [`debug.setstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack) | Set a value on the stack |
| [`debug.setupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue) | Set an upvalue in a function |
| [`debug.validlevel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel) | Check if a stack level is valid |

[Terminology](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#terminology)

-----------------------------------------------------------

### [Constants](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#constants)

Values embedded directly in the function's bytecode. These include:

*   String literals
*   Numbers
*   Booleans
*   `nil`

### [Upvalues](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#upvalues)

Variables captured from the enclosing scope. When a function references a variable from outside its own scope, that variable becomes an upvalue.

### [Protos](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#protos)

Nested function definitions within a function. These are the "prototypes" of inner functions.

### [Stack](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#stack)

The call stack containing local variables and temporary values for the current execution context.

[crypt.random\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random)
[debug.getcallstack\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#available-functions)
[Terminology](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#terminology)
[Constants](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#constants)
[Upvalues](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#upvalues)
[Protos](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug#protos)

# Volt Documentation

Closures
========

The **Closures** library allows for viewing info about a closures origin and allowing the manipulation of said closure.

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#overview)

--------------------------------------------------------

This library provides tools to:

*   **Inspect** closures to determine their type and origin
*   **Modify** closures by hooking or replacing them
*   **Create** new closures with specific properties

[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#available-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [`checkcaller`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller) | Check if the current call is from volt |
| [`clonefunction`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction) | Create a copy of a function |
| [`getfunctionhash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash) | Get the hash of a function's bytecode |
| [`hookfunction`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction) | Replace a function with another |
| [`hookmetamethod`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod) | Hook a metatable metamethod |
| [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure) | Check if a function is a C closure |
| [`isexecutorclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure) | Check if a function is from volt |
| [`isfunctionhooked`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked) | Check if a function has been hooked |
| [`islclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure) | Check if a function is a Luau closure |
| [`isnewcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure) | Check if a function is a newcclosure |
| [`newcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure) | Wrap a Luau function as a C closure |
| [`newlclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure) | Wrap a C closure as a Luau closure |
| [`restorefunction`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction) | Restore a hooked function to its original |
| [`setstackhidden`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden) | Hide a function from stack traces |

[Closure Types](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#closure-types)

------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two main types of closures:

### [C Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#c-closures)

Functions implemented in C/C++. These are typically:

*   Built-in Lua functions like `print`, `type`
*   Roblox API methods
*   Majority of custom functions

### [Luau Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#luau-closures)

Functions written in Luau. These are typically:

*   User-defined functions
*   Game Script functions

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace)
[checkcaller\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller)

### On this page

[Overview](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#overview)
[Available Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#available-functions)
[Closure Types](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#closure-types)
[C Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures#c-closures)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

create\_comm\_channel
=====================

Creates a communication channel for sending messages between actors.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    create_comm_channel(name: string?) -> (string, Channel)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `name` | `string` | (Optional) Name for the channel |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The channel identifier |
| `Channel` | The channel object |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`create_comm_channel` creates a new communication channel that can be used to send and receive messages between actors and the main thread.

[Channel Object](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#channel-object)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property/Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Event` | Signal to connect for receiving |
| `Fire(...)` | Send a message through the channel |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    
    -- Listen for messages
    channel.Event:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    -- Send to an actor
    run_on_actor(someActor, [[\
        local channelId = ...\
        local channel = get_comm_channel(channelId)\
        channel:Fire("Hello from actor!")\
    ]], id)

[Bidirectional Communication](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#bidirectional-communication)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Main thread
    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    channel.Event:Connect(function(response)
        print("Actor responded:", response)
    end)
    
    -- Actor sends back
    run_on_actor(actor, [[\
        local id = ...\
        local channel = get_comm_channel(id)\
        channel:Fire("Message received!")\
    ]], id)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`get_comm_channel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel)
     - Retrieve a channel
*   [`run_on_actor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor)
     - Run code on an actor

[Actors\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)
[get\_comm\_channel\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Cache](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache)

cache.invalidate
================

Removes an instance from the reference cache.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    cache.invalidate(instance: Instance) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to invalidate |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`cache.invalidate` removes an instance from the internal reference cache. The next access to this instance will create a new reference.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    
    -- Store a reference
    local ref1 = part
    
    -- Invalidate the cache
    cache.invalidate(part)
    
    -- New reference is created
    local ref2 = workspace.Part
    
    print(ref1 == ref2) -- May be false

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------

*   Used for advanced instance manipulation
*   Affects how references are tracked

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`cache.replace`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace)
     - Replace cached instance
*   [`cache.iscached`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached)
     - Check if cached

[Cache\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache)
[cache.iscached\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#example)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#notes)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Cache](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache)

cache.iscached
==============

Checks if an instance is in the reference cache.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    cache.iscached(instance: Instance) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the instance is cached |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`cache.iscached` checks whether an instance currently exists in the reference cache.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    
    if cache.iscached(part) then
        print("Part is cached")
    else
        print("Part is not cached")
    end
    
    -- After invalidation
    cache.invalidate(part)
    print(cache.iscached(part)) -- false

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`cache.replace`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace)
     - Replace cached instance
*   [`cache.invalidate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate)
     - Remove from cache

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace)

# Volt Documentation

[Cache](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache)

cache.replace
=============

Replaces a cached instance reference with another.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------

    cache.replace(instance: Instance, replacement: Instance) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to replace |
| `replacement` | `Instance` | The replacement instance |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

`cache.replace` replaces a cached instance reference with another instance. All existing references to the original instance will now point to the replacement.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    local original = workspace.Part
    local replacement = Instance.new("Part")
    replacement.Name = "FakePart"
    
    -- Replace the cached reference
    cache.replace(original, replacement)
    
    -- Now any access to the original returns the replacement
    print(workspace.Part.Name) -- "FakePart"

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#notes)

-------------------------------------------------------

*   Use with caution as this affects all references
*   The original instance still exists

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`cache.invalidate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/invalidate)
     - Remove from cache
*   [`cache.iscached`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached)
     - Check if cached

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/iscached)
[Closures\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#example)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache/replace#notes)

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

checkcaller
===========

Returns whether the current function was called by volt.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    checkcaller() -> boolean

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if called from volt thread, `false` otherwise |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`checkcaller` returns a boolean indicating whether the current function was invoked from volt's own thread. This is useful for differentiating between your own calls and those made by the game.

When you hook a game function, both your code and the game will trigger it. Use `checkcaller` to determine whether to run custom logic or pass through to the original.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local old
    old = hookfunction(game.HttpGet, function(self, url, ...)
        if checkcaller() then
            -- Call is from our script, allow it
            return old(self, url, ...)
        end
    
        -- Call is from the game, we can block or modify it
        print("Game tried to fetch:", url)
        return old(self, url, ...)
    end)
    
    -- This will pass checkcaller() because we're calling it
    local result = game:HttpGet("https://example.com")

[Closures\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)
[clonefunction\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller#example)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

get\_comm\_channel
==================

Retrieves an existing communication channel by its identifier.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    get_comm_channel(id: string) -> Channel

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `id` | `string` | The channel identifier |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Channel` | The channel object |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`get_comm_channel` retrieves a communication channel that was created with `create_comm_channel`. This is typically used inside an actor to get a reference to a channel created on the main thread.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- On main thread
    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    channel.Event:Connect(print)
    
    -- Inside actor (via run_on_actor)
    run_on_actor(actor, [[\
        local channelId = ...\
        local channel = get_comm_channel(channelId)\
        channel:Fire("Hello from actor!")\
    ]], id)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   The channel ID is passed from the main thread to the actor
*   Use this inside actors to communicate back to the main thread

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/get_comm_channel#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`create_comm_channel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel)
     - Create a channel
*   [`run_on_actor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor)
     - Run code on an actor

# Volt Documentation

[Drawing](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing)

cleardrawcache
==============

Removes all cached drawing objects.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    cleardrawcache() -> void

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`cleardrawcache` removes all drawing objects that have been created. This is useful for cleanup when you want to clear all visual overlays at once.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create several drawings
    local drawings = {}
    for i = 1, 10 do
        local circle = Drawing.new("Circle")
        circle.Position = Vector2.new(100 * i, 100)
        circle.Radius = 50
        circle.Visible = true
        table.insert(drawings, circle)
    end
    
    -- Later, clear everything at once
    cleardrawcache()
    -- All 10 circles are now removed

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#use-cases)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Script cleanup**: Remove all drawings when a script ends
*   **Reset**: Clear all visuals before recreating them
*   **Performance**: Free memory from unused drawings

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/cleardrawcache#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   This removes ALL drawings, not just ones you created
*   Use with caution in multi-script environments
*   Individual drawings can be removed with `:Remove()`

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.decrypt
=============

Decrypts data using a specified algorithm and key.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.decrypt(data: string, key: string, iv: string?, algorithm: string?) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The encrypted data |
| `key` | `string` | The decryption key |
| `iv` | `string` | (Optional) Initialization vector |
| `algorithm` | `string` | (Optional) Algorithm, defaults to "AES-CBC" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The decrypted data |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.decrypt` decrypts data that was encrypted with `crypt.encrypt` using the same algorithm and key.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    local key = crypt.generatekey()
    local original = "Hello, World!"
    
    -- Encrypt and decrypt
    local encrypted = crypt.encrypt(original, key)
    local decrypted = crypt.decrypt(encrypted, key)
    
    print(decrypted) -- "Hello, World!"

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.encrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt)
     - Encrypt data
*   [`crypt.generatekey`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey)
     - Generate a key

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

getactorstates
==============

Returns all active LuaStateProxy objects.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    getactorstates() -> {LuaStateProxy}

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{LuaStateProxy}` | Array of all active LuaStateProxy objects |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getactorstates` returns all active `LuaStateProxy` objects in the game. This includes both actor states and the main game state. Each `LuaStateProxy` represents a unique Lua execution environment.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local states = getactorstates()
    print("Total Lua states:", #states)
    
    for i, state in ipairs(states) do
        print(i, "State ID:", state.Id, "Is Actor:", state.IsActorState)
    end

[Filter Actor States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#filter-actor-states)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local states = getactorstates()
    local actorStates = {}
    
    for _, state in ipairs(states) do
        if state.IsActorState then
            table.insert(actorStates, state)
        end
    end
    
    print("Actor states:", #actorStates)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate)
     - Get LuaStateProxy for a specific actor or script
*   [`getgamestate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getgamestate)
     - Get the default game Lua state
*   [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors)
     - Get all Actor instances

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

clonefunction
=============

Creates a copy of the given function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    clonefunction(func: function) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to clone |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A copy of the original function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`clonefunction` creates an independent copy of a function. The cloned function behaves identically to the original but is a separate entity. This is particularly useful when you need to keep a reference to the original behavior before hooking.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Clone a function before hooking it
    local originalPrint = clonefunction(print)
    
    -- Now hook the original
    hookfunction(print, function(...)
        originalPrint("[HOOKED]", ...)
    end)
    
    -- The clone still works as the original
    originalPrint("This bypasses the hook")
    
    -- The hooked version adds prefix
    print("This goes through the hook") -- Output: [HOOKED] This goes through the hook

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   The cloned function shares the same upvalues as the original
*   For C closures, the clone wraps the same underlying C function
*   Cloning is useful for preserving original behavior during hooks

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction#aliases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `clonefunc`

\

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash)

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getcallstack
==================

Gets the current call stack.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getcallstack(level: number?) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `level` | `number` | (Optional) Starting level, default 1 |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of call stack entries |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getcallstack` returns information about the current call stack, including function names and source locations.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local function innerFunc()
        local stack = debug.getcallstack()
        for i, entry in ipairs(stack) do
            print(i, entry.name or "anonymous", entry.source)
        end
    end
    
    local function outerFunc()
        innerFunc()
    end
    
    outerFunc()

[Entry Fields](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#entry-fields)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `name` | Function name |
| `source` | Source file/script |
| `line` | Current line number |
| `func` | The function itself |

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getinfo`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo)
     - Get info for specific level
*   [`debug.validlevel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel)
     - Check if level is valid

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

getfunctionhash
===============

Returns a hash of the function's bytecode.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    getfunctionhash(func: function) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to hash |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | A hash string representing the function's bytecode |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getfunctionhash` generates a unique hash based on the function's compiled bytecode. Functions with identical source code will produce the same hash, making this useful for identifying and comparing functions.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function testFunc()
        return 1 + 1
    end
    
    local hash = getfunctionhash(testFunc)
    print(hash) -- Output: something like "a1b2c3d4..."
    
    -- Same code produces same hash
    local function testFunc2()
        return 1 + 1
    end
    
    print(getfunctionhash(testFunc2) == hash) -- true

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only works with Luau closures (not C closures)
*   Slight changes in function bytecode will alter the returned hash

[clonefunction\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/clonefunction)
[hookfunction\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash#description)

[Encoding](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding)

base64decode
============

Decodes a Base64 encoded string.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    base64decode(data: string) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The Base64 encoded string |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The decoded binary data |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`base64decode` converts a Base64 encoded string back to its original binary form.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local encoded = "SGVsbG8sIFdvcmxkIQ=="
    local decoded = base64decode(encoded)
    print(decoded) -- "Hello, World!"

[Round-trip Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#round-trip-example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local original = "This is a test message!"
    
    -- Encode then decode
    local encoded = base64encode(original)
    local decoded = base64decode(encoded)
    
    print(original == decoded) -- true

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#use-cases)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **API responses**: Decode Base64 data from web APIs
*   **Embedded data**: Extract binary data from encoded strings
*   **Deserialization**: Decode stored or transmitted data

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`base64encode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode)
     - Encode to Base64

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode#aliases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `base64_decode`

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

setsimulationradius
===================

Sets the player's network simulation radius.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    setsimulationradius(radius: number, maxRadius: number?) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `radius` | `number` | The simulation radius |
| `maxRadius` | `number` | (Optional) Maximum radius |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setsimulationradius` sets how far from the player physics simulation ownership extends. This affects network ownership of parts.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Set maximum simulation radius
    setsimulationradius(math.huge, math.huge)
    
    -- Now the player owns physics simulation for distant objects

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Higher values give you ownership of more physics objects
*   Server can override network ownership
*   Used for physics manipulation

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isnetworkowner`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner)
     - Check ownership

[setscriptable\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity)

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

readfile
========

Reads the contents of a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    readfile(path: string) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The file contents |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`readfile` reads and returns the entire contents of a file as a string.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Write and then read a file
    writefile("message.txt", "Hello, World!")
    local content = readfile("message.txt")
    print(content) -- "Hello, World!"

[Reading JSON](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#reading-json)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    
    -- Write JSON data
    local data = {name = "Player", score = 100}
    writefile("save.json", HttpService:JSONEncode(data))
    
    -- Read and parse JSON
    local content = readfile("save.json")
    local loaded = HttpService:JSONDecode(content)
    print(loaded.name, loaded.score) -- "Player" 100

[Error Handling](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#error-handling)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeRead(path)
        local success, result = pcall(readfile, path)
        if success then
            return result
        else
            warn("Failed to read:", result)
            return nil
        end
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`writefile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile)
     - Write to a file
*   [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile)
     - Check if file exists
*   [`loadfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile)
     - Load Lua file as function

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile)

# Volt Documentation

[Drawing](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing)

getrenderproperty
=================

Gets a property value from a drawing object.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    getrenderproperty(drawing: Drawing, property: string) -> any

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `drawing` | `Drawing` | The drawing object |
| `property` | `string` | The property name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The value of the property |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getrenderproperty` retrieves the current value of a property on a drawing object. This is an alternative to directly accessing properties.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local circle = Drawing.new("Circle")
    circle.Position = Vector2.new(500, 500)
    circle.Radius = 100
    circle.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    circle.Visible = true
    
    -- Get properties using getrenderproperty
    local pos = getrenderproperty(circle, "Position")
    local radius = getrenderproperty(circle, "Radius")
    local color = getrenderproperty(circle, "Color")
    
    print(pos)    -- 500, 500
    print(radius) -- 100
    print(color)  -- 1, 0, 0

[Properties by Type](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#properties-by-type)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Circle](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#circle)

*   `Position` (Vector2)
*   `Radius` (number)
*   `Filled` (boolean)
*   `Thickness` (number)

### [Line](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#line)

*   `From` (Vector2)
*   `To` (Vector2)
*   `Thickness` (number)

### [Text](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#text)

*   `Position` (Vector2)
*   `Text` (string)
*   `Size` (number)
*   `Font` (Drawing.Fonts)
*   `Center` (boolean)
*   `Outline` (boolean)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`setrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty)
     - Set a property
*   [`isrenderobj`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj)
     - Check if value is a drawing

[Encoding](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding)

base64encode
============

Encodes data to Base64 format.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    base64encode(data: string) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The binary data to encode |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The Base64 encoded string |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`base64encode` converts binary data into a Base64 encoded string that contains only ASCII characters.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local data = "Hello, World!"
    local encoded = base64encode(data)
    print(encoded) -- "SGVsbG8sIFdvcmxkIQ=="

[Encoding Binary Data](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#encoding-binary-data)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Encode binary data (like file contents)
    local binaryData = "\0\1\2\3\255\254"
    local encoded = base64encode(binaryData)
    print(encoded) -- Safe ASCII string

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#use-cases)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Data transmission**: Send binary data over text protocols
*   **Storage**: Store binary data in JSON or other text formats
*   **Obfuscation**: Light obfuscation of string data

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`base64decode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64decode)
     - Decode from Base64

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode#aliases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `base64_encode`
