# Volt Documentation

[Environment](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

filtergc
========

Filters objects in the garbage collector based on specified criteria.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    filtergc(type: string, options: table) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | `string` | The type of object to find ("function" or "table") |
| `options` | `table` | Filter options |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of matching objects |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`filtergc` efficiently searches through garbage-collected objects with specific filter criteria. This is more performant than manually iterating through `getgc()`.

[Function Filter Options](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#function-filter-options)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Option | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Name` | `string` | Match function name |
| `Constants` | `table` | Match constants in function |
| `Upvalues` | `table` | Match upvalue values |
| `IgnoreExecutor` | `boolean` | Exclude volt functions |

[Table Filter Options](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#table-filter-options)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Option | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Keys` | `table` | Match table keys |
| `Values` | `table` | Match table values |
| `KeyValuePairs` | `table` | Match key-value pairs |
| `Metatable` | `table` | Match metatable |

[Example: Find Function by Name](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#example-find-function-by-name)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local functions = filtergc("function", {
        Name = "targetFunction"
    })
    
    for _, func in ipairs(functions) do
        print("Found:", func)
    end

[Example: Find Function by Constants](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#example-find-function-by-constants)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local functions = filtergc("function", {
        Constants = {"SomeUniqueString", "AnotherString"}
    })

[Example: Find Table by Keys](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#example-find-table-by-keys)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local tables = filtergc("table", {
        Keys = {"Health", "MaxHealth", "Damage"}
    })
    
    for _, tbl in ipairs(tables) do
        print("Found table with game stats")
    end

[Example: Ignore Volt Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#example-ignore-volt-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local gameFunctions = filtergc("function", {
        Name = "Update",
        IgnoreExecutor = true
    })

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getgc`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc)
     - Get all GC objects

[Environment\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)
[getgc\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc)

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.encrypt
=============

Encrypts data using a specified algorithm and key.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.encrypt(data: string, key: string, iv: string?, algorithm: string?) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The data to encrypt |
| `key` | `string` | The encryption key |
| `iv` | `string` | (Optional) Initialization vector |
| `algorithm` | `string` | (Optional) Algorithm, defaults to "AES-CBC" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The encrypted data |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.encrypt` encrypts the provided data using the specified algorithm and key. The result is typically Base64-encoded.

[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#supported-algorithms)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `AES-CBC` (default)
*   `AES-GCM`
*   `AES-CTR`

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    local key = crypt.generatekey()
    local data = "Secret message"
    
    -- Encrypt with default algorithm
    local encrypted = crypt.encrypt(data, key)
    print("Encrypted:", encrypted)
    
    -- Decrypt to verify
    local decrypted = crypt.decrypt(encrypted, key)
    print("Decrypted:", decrypted)

[With Custom IV](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#with-custom-iv)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local key = crypt.generatekey()
    local iv = crypt.generatebytes(16)
    local data = "Secret message"
    
    local encrypted = crypt.encrypt(data, key, iv, "AES-CBC")
    local decrypted = crypt.decrypt(encrypted, key, iv, "AES-CBC")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.decrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt)
     - Decrypt data
*   [`crypt.generatekey`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey)
     - Generate a key

[crypt.decrypt\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt)
[crypt.generatebytes\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes)

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#description)
[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt#supported-algorithms)

[Drawing](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing)

isrenderobj
===========

Checks if a value is a drawing object.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    isrenderobj(value: any) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `value` | `any` | The value to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the value is a drawing object |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isrenderobj` determines whether a given value is a valid drawing object created by `Drawing.new()`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    local circle = Drawing.new("Circle")
    local normalTable = {}
    local number = 123
    
    print(isrenderobj(circle))      -- true
    print(isrenderobj(normalTable)) -- false
    print(isrenderobj(number))      -- false
    print(isrenderobj(nil))         -- false

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#use-cases)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Validation**: Verify that a value is a drawing before manipulating it
*   **Cleanup**: Filter drawing objects from a mixed table
*   **Debugging**: Identify the type of unknown values

[Example: Safe Removal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#example-safe-removal)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeRemove(obj)
        if isrenderobj(obj) then
            obj:Remove()
            return true
        end
        return false
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty)
     - Get a drawing property
*   [`setrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty)
     - Set a drawing property

\

# Volt Documentation

[Encoding](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding)

lz4compress
===========

Compresses data using the LZ4 algorithm.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    lz4compress(data: string) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The data to compress |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The LZ4 compressed data |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`lz4compress` compresses a string using the LZ4 compression algorithm. LZ4 is optimized for speed over compression ratio, making it ideal for real-time applications.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local data = string.rep("Hello, World! ", 1000)
    print("Original size:", #data) -- 14000
    
    local compressed = lz4compress(data)
    print("Compressed size:", #compressed) -- Much smaller
    
    local decompressed = lz4decompress(compressed, #data)
    print(data == decompressed) -- true

[Compression Ratio](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#compression-ratio)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LZ4 works best with:

*   Repetitive data
*   Text with patterns
*   Structured data

    -- High compression (repetitive data)
    local repetitive = string.rep("AAAA", 10000)
    local comp1 = lz4compress(repetitive)
    print(#comp1 / #repetitive) -- Very small ratio
    
    -- Lower compression (random data)
    local random = ""
    for i = 1, 1000 do
        random = random .. string.char(math.random(0, 255))
    end
    local comp2 = lz4compress(random)
    print(#comp2 / #random) -- Closer to 1

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`lz4decompress`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress)
     - Decompress LZ4 data

[base64encode\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/base64encode)
[lz4decompress\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#example)
[Compression Ratio](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#compression-ratio)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

saveplace
=========

Saves the current place to a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    saveplace(filename: string?) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `filename` | `string` | (Optional) Output file name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`saveplace` is a shorthand for `saveinstance` that saves the entire game to a file.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Save with default name
    saveplace()
    
    -- Save with custom name
    saveplace("MyGame.rbxl")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Saves to the workspace folder
*   Equivalent to `saveinstance({FilePath = filename})`

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`saveinstance`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance)
     - Full save with options

\

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy.Event
===================

Generic event for communication between Lua states.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    state.Event: VoltSignal

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy.Event` is a `VoltSignal` property that allows communication between different Lua states. You can connect handlers to listen for events and fire events to send messages to other states.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    
    -- Listen for events
    state.Event:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    -- Fire an event
    state.Event:Fire("Hello from this state!")

[Cross-State Communication](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#cross-state-communication)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local gameState = getgamestate()
    local actorState = getluastate(someActor)
    
    -- Listen on game state
    gameState.Event:Connect(function(message, senderId)
        print("Game state received:", message, "from state", senderId)
    end)
    
    -- Fire from actor state
    actorState.Event:Fire("Hello from actor!", actorState.Id)

[Broadcast to All States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#broadcast-to-all-states)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local states = getactorstates()
    
    -- Broadcast to all actor states
    for _, state in ipairs(states) do
        if state.IsActorState then
            state.Event:Fire("Broadcast message")
        end
    end

[Related Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#related-properties)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`LuaStateProxy.Id`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id)
     - State identifier for message routing
*   [`VoltSignal`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)
     - Signal implementation documentation

[LuaStateProxy\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)
[LuaStateProxy:Execute\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#syntax)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#example)
[Cross-State Communication](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event#cross-state-communication)

# Volt Documentation

[Environment](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

getgc
=====

Returns a table of all objects tracked by the garbage collector.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    getgc(includeTables?: boolean) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `includeTables` | `boolean?` | Whether to include tables (default: false) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of all GC-tracked objects |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`getgc` returns all objects currently tracked by Luau's garbage collector. This is useful for finding specific functions, tables, or other objects in memory.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get all functions in memory
    for _, obj in ipairs(getgc()) do
        if type(obj) == "function" then
            print("Found function:", obj)
        end
    end

[Finding Specific Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#finding-specific-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find a function by its constants
    local function findFunction(targetString)
        for _, obj in ipairs(getgc()) do
            if type(obj) == "function" then
                local constants = debug.getconstants(obj)
                for _, const in ipairs(constants) do
                    if const == targetString then
                        return obj
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    
    local targetFunc = findFunction("SomeUniqueString")

[Including Tables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#including-tables)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get all tables (slower, more results)
    local allObjects = getgc(true)
    
    for _, obj in ipairs(allObjects) do
        if type(obj) == "table" and obj.SpecialKey then
            print("Found target table!")
        end
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   Without `includeTables`, only functions and other non-table objects are returned
*   Including tables can be slow due to the large number of tables in memory
*   Consider using `filtergc` for more targeted searches

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`filtergc`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc)
     - Filter objects with conditions

[filtergc\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/filtergc)
[getgenv\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#example)
[Finding Specific Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgc#finding-specific-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[oth](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)

get\_original\_thread
=====================

Returns the original thread associated with the hook, or nil if not in a hook thread.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    get_original_thread() -> thread?

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `thread?` | The original thread, or nil if not in a hook thread |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`get_original_thread` returns the original thread that called the hooked function. This is useful for accessing thread-local data or resuming execution on the original thread.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalPrint = oth.hook(print, function(...)
        local originalThread = get_original_thread()
        if originalThread then
            print("Original thread:", originalThread)
            print("Arguments:", ...)
        end
        return originalPrint(...)
    end)
    
    print("Test")

[Thread Context](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#thread-context)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalFunc = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        local originalThread = get_original_thread()
        
        if originalThread then
            -- We're in a hook thread
            print("Hook thread, original:", originalThread)
            -- Access thread-local data if needed
        else
            -- Not in a hook thread
            print("Not in hook thread")
        end
        
        return originalFunc(...)
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns `nil` if not currently executing in a hook thread
*   The returned thread is the one that originally called the hooked function
*   Useful for thread-local data access or debugging

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`oth.hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)
     - Create a hook
*   [`oth.is_hook_thread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread)
     - Check if in a hook thread

[oth\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)
[oth.get\_root\_callback\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback)

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread#example)

# Volt Documentation

[oth](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)

oth.get\_root\_callback
=======================

Returns the original function, even after multiple hooks.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    oth.get_root_callback(target: function) -> function?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `target` | `function` | The hooked function |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function?` | The original function, or nil if not found |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`oth.get_root_callback` returns the original function that was hooked, even if multiple hooks have been applied. This allows you to bypass all hooks and call the true original function.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook a function multiple times
    local hook1 = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        print("Hook 1")
        return hook1(...)
    end)
    
    local hook2 = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        print("Hook 2")
        return hook2(...)
    end)
    
    -- Get the original, bypassing all hooks
    local original = oth.get_root_callback(someCFunction)
    original("test") -- Calls the true original, bypassing both hooks

[Bypass All Hooks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#bypass-all-hooks)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local hookedFunc = oth.hook(print, function(...)
        print("[HOOKED]", ...)
    end)
    
    -- Get original to bypass hook
    local original = oth.get_root_callback(print)
    if original then
        original("Direct call") -- Bypasses the hook
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns `nil` if the function was never hooked or is not a C function
*   Always returns the true original, regardless of how many hooks exist
*   Useful for completely bypassing all hook layers

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`oth.hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)
     - Create a hook
*   [`oth.unhook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook)
     - Remove a hook

[get\_original\_thread\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread)
[oth.hook\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#example)
[Bypass All Hooks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#bypass-all-hooks)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#notes)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getscripts
==========

Returns all scripts in the game.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    getscripts() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of all scripts |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getscripts` returns all script instances in the game, including LocalScripts, Scripts, and ModuleScripts.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local scripts = getscripts()
    print("Total scripts:", #scripts)
    
    -- Count by type
    local counts = {LocalScript = 0, ModuleScript = 0, Script = 0}
    for _, script in ipairs(scripts) do
        local class = script.ClassName
        counts[class] = (counts[class] or 0) + 1
    end
    
    for class, count in pairs(counts) do
        print(class, count)
    end

[Finding Specific Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#finding-specific-scripts)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function findScript(name)
        for _, script in ipairs(getscripts()) do
            if script.Name == name then
                return script
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    
    local mainScript = findScript("MainLocalScript")
    if mainScript then
        print("Found:", mainScript:GetFullName())
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getrunningscripts`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getrunningscripts)
     - Get only running scripts
*   [`getloadedmodules`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules)
     - Get only loaded modules

[getscripthash\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash)
[getsenv\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts#example)

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

setthreadidentity
=================

Sets the current thread's identity level.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    setthreadidentity(identity: number) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `identity` | `number` | The identity level (1-8) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setthreadidentity` changes the identity level of the current thread, which affects what APIs and properties are accessible.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Check current identity
    print("Before:", getthreadidentity())
    
    -- Elevate identity
    setthreadidentity(8)
    
    print("After:", getthreadidentity())
    
    -- Perform restricted operations here

[Safe Identity Change](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#safe-identity-change)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function withIdentity(level, callback)
        local original = getthreadidentity()
        setthreadidentity(level)
        
        local success, result = pcall(callback)
        
        setthreadidentity(original)
        
        if not success then
            error(result)
        end
        
        return result
    end
    
    -- Use elevated identity temporarily
    local result = withIdentity(8, function()
        -- Restricted operations here
        return "done"
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Higher identity gives more permissions
*   Some operations require specific identity levels
*   Always restore original identity when done

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getthreadidentity`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getthreadidentity)
     - Get current identity

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setthreadidentity#aliases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `setidentity`
*   `setthreadcontext`

# Volt Documentation

[Drawing](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing)

setrenderproperty
=================

Sets a property value on a drawing object.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    setrenderproperty(drawing: Drawing, property: string, value: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `drawing` | `Drawing` | The drawing object |
| `property` | `string` | The property name |
| `value` | `any` | The new value |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setrenderproperty` sets the value of a property on a drawing object. This is an alternative to directly assigning properties.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local text = Drawing.new("Text")
    
    -- Set properties using setrenderproperty
    setrenderproperty(text, "Position", Vector2.new(100, 100))
    setrenderproperty(text, "Text", "Hello, World!")
    setrenderproperty(text, "Size", 24)
    setrenderproperty(text, "Color", Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
    setrenderproperty(text, "Outline", true)
    setrenderproperty(text, "Visible", true)

[Batch Updates](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#batch-updates)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function updateDrawing(drawing, properties)
        for property, value in pairs(properties) do
            setrenderproperty(drawing, property, value)
        end
    end
    
    local circle = Drawing.new("Circle")
    updateDrawing(circle, {
        Position = Vector2.new(400, 300),
        Radius = 50,
        Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0),
        Filled = true,
        Visible = true
    })

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/setrenderproperty#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getrenderproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/getrenderproperty)
     - Get a property
*   [`isrenderobj`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/drawing/isrenderobj)
     - Check if value is a drawing

crypt.generatebytes
===================

Generates cryptographically secure random bytes.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.generatebytes(length: number) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes#parameters)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `length` | `number` | Number of bytes to generate |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | Random bytes (raw string) |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.generatebytes` generates cryptographically secure random bytes, useful for creating initialization vectors, salts, or other random data.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Generate 16 bytes for an IV
    local iv = crypt.generatebytes(16)

    local salt = crypt.generatebytes(32)

# Volt Documentation

[Encoding](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding)

lz4decompress
=============

Decompresses LZ4 compressed data.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    lz4decompress(data: string, size: number) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The LZ4 compressed data |
| `size` | `number` | The original uncompressed size |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The decompressed data |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`lz4decompress` decompresses data that was compressed with `lz4compress`. You must provide the original uncompressed size for the decompression to work correctly.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local original = "This is the original data that will be compressed!"
    local originalSize = #original
    
    -- Compress
    local compressed = lz4compress(original)
    
    -- Decompress (need to know original size)
    local decompressed = lz4decompress(compressed, originalSize)
    
    print(original == decompressed) -- true

[Storing Size with Data](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#storing-size-with-data)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When storing compressed data, you should also store the original size:

    local function compressWithSize(data)
        local compressed = lz4compress(data)
        -- Prepend the size as a 4-byte integer
        local size = #data
        return string.pack("<I4", size) .. compressed
    end
    
    local function decompressWithSize(data)
        local size = string.unpack("<I4", data)
        local compressed = data:sub(5)
        return lz4decompress(compressed, size)
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   The size parameter must match the original data size exactly
*   Providing wrong size may cause errors or corrupted output

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`lz4compress`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress)
     - Compress with LZ4

[lz4compress\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4compress)
[Environment\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/encoding/lz4decompress#example)

# Volt Documentation

[WebSocket](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

WebSocket:Close
===============

Closes the WebSocket connection.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    WebSocket:Close() -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This method takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------

This method does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

`WebSocket:Close` terminates the WebSocket connection. After closing, the `OnClose` event will fire and no more messages can be sent or received.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    
    ws.OnClose:Connect(function()
        print("Connection closed")
    end)
    
    -- Use the connection
    ws:Send("Hello!")
    
    -- Close after 10 seconds
    task.wait(10)
    ws:Close()

[Cleanup Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#cleanup-pattern)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    
    local function cleanup()
        if ws then
            ws:Close()
            ws = nil
        end
    end
    
    -- Close on script end or when done
    cleanup()

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------

*   Connection cannot be reopened after closing
*   `OnClose` event fires after calling Close
*   Safe to call multiple times

[Related](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close#related)

-------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`WebSocket.connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)
     - Create connection
*   [`OnClose`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose)
     - Close event

[WebSocket\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)
[WebSocket.connect\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)

# Volt Documentation

[VoltSignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

VoltSignal:Connect
==================

Connects a handler function to the signal.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    VoltSignal:Connect(f: function) -> VoltConnection

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `f` | `function` | The handler function to call when the signal fires |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `VoltConnection` | A connection object that can be used to disconnect |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`VoltSignal:Connect` registers a function to be called whenever the signal is fired. The function will receive any arguments passed to `Fire`. Returns a `VoltConnection` that can be used to disconnect the handler.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    -- Connect a handler
    local connection = signal:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    -- Fire the signal
    signal:Fire("Hello, World!")
    -- Output: Received: Hello, World!
    
    -- Disconnect when done
    connection:Disconnect()

[Multiple Connections](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#multiple-connections)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    signal:Connect(function(value)
        print("Handler 1:", value)
    end)
    
    signal:Connect(function(value)
        print("Handler 2:", value * 2)
    end)
    
    signal:Fire(10)
    -- Output:
    -- Handler 1: 10
    -- Handler 2: 20

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`VoltSignal.new`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new)
     - Create a signal
*   [`VoltConnection:Disconnect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect)
     - Disconnect a handler

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect)

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

getnamecallmethod
=================

Gets the method name being called in a `__namecall` hook.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    getnamecallmethod() -> string

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The method name being called |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getnamecallmethod` returns the name of the method being called when inside a `__namecall` metamethod hook. This is essential for filtering which method calls to intercept.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
        
        if method == "Kick" then
            return -- Block kick
        end
        
        if method == "FireServer" then
            print("FireServer called on:", self)
        end
        
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))

[Common Methods to Hook](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#common-methods-to-hook)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Method | Object | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `FireServer` | RemoteEvent | Client to server communication |
| `InvokeServer` | RemoteFunction | Client to server with return |
| `Kick` | Player | Kick the player |
| `Destroy` | Instance | Destroy an instance |
| `GetService` | ServiceProvider | Get a service |

[Filtering Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#filtering-example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local blockedMethods = {"Kick", "Ban", "Disconnect"}
    
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
        
        if table.find(blockedMethods, method) then
            warn("Blocked:", method)
            return
        end
        
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only works inside `__namecall` hooks
*   Returns the exact method name as a string
*   Case-sensitive

[Metatable\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)
[getrawmetatable\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#example)
[Common Methods to Hook](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod#common-methods-to-hook)

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy:Execute
=====================

Schedules code execution on this Lua state.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    state:Execute(source: string, ...: any) -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `source` | `string` | The Lua code to execute |
| `...` | `any` | Arguments passed to the script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This method does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy:Execute` schedules code execution on the Lua state. The code string will be executed in the context of that state, and any additional arguments will be passed to the script via varargs (`...`).

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    
    state:Execute([[\
        print("Executed on state:", ...)\
    ]], "arg1", "arg2")

[Execute on Actor State](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#execute-on-actor-state)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local actor = Instance.new("Actor")
    actor.Parent = workspace
    
    local actorState = getluastate(actor)
    actorState:Execute([[\
        print("Running on actor state!")\
        print("Arguments:", ...)\
    ]], "test", 123)

[Pass Data to State](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#pass-data-to-state)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local gameState = getgamestate()
    
    local data = {
        message = "Hello",
        value = 42
    }
    
    gameState:Execute([[\
        local data = ...\
        print("Message:", data.message)\
        print("Value:", data.value)\
    ]], data)

[Setup Code on New States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#setup-code-on-new-states)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_state_created.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        local state = getluastate(actor)
        
        state:Execute([[\
            -- Setup code runs before any scripts\
            print("State initialized!")\
            _G.setupComplete = true\
        ]])
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Code executes asynchronously on the target state
*   Arguments are passed via varargs (`...`)
*   Useful for injecting code or setting up state before scripts run

[Related Methods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute#related-methods)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`LuaStateProxy:GetActors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors)
     - Get actors for this state
*   [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate)
     - Get state for an actor

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event)

# Volt Documentation

[oth](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)

oth.is\_hook\_thread
====================

Returns true if the current thread is a hook thread.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    oth.is_hook_thread() -> boolean

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if running in a hook thread, false otherwise |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`oth.is_hook_thread` checks whether the current code is executing within a hook thread created by `oth.hook`. This allows you to detect hook context and behave differently.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalPrint = oth.hook(print, function(...)
        if oth.is_hook_thread() then
            print("[HOOK THREAD]", ...)
        else
            print("[MAIN THREAD]", ...)
        end
        return originalPrint(...)
    end)
    
    print("Test") -- Output: [HOOK THREAD] Test

[Conditional Behavior](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#conditional-behavior)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalFunc = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        if oth.is_hook_thread() then
            -- Running in hook thread
            print("Hook context detected")
            -- Do hook-specific logic
        end
        return originalFunc(...)
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns `true` only when executing within a hook created by `oth.hook`
*   Returns `false` on the main thread or in other contexts
*   Useful for implementing hook-specific behavior

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`oth.hook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)
     - Create a hook
*   [`get_original_thread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_original_thread)
     - Get the original thread

[oth.hook\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook)
[oth.unhook\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread#description)

# Volt Documentation

[oth](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth)

oth.hook
========

Secure alternative to `hookfunction` for C functions. Hooks are executed on separate threads.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------

    oth.hook(target: function, hook: function) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `target` | `function` | The C function to hook |
| `hook` | `function` | The replacement function |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#returns)

------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A reference to the original function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------

`oth.hook` replaces the target C function with your hook function. Unlike `hookfunction`, hooks are executed on separate threads, providing better isolation and safety. The function returns a reference to the original, allowing you to call it from within your hook.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#example)

------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook a C function
    local originalFunc = oth.hook(someCFunction, function(...)
        print("Hooked call:", ...)
        return originalFunc(...)
    end)
    
    -- Call the original
    originalFunc("test")

[Thread Safety](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#thread-safety)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local originalPrint = oth.hook(print, function(...)
        -- This runs on a separate thread
        if oth.is_hook_thread() then
            print("[HOOK THREAD]", ...)
        end
        return originalPrint(...)
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#notes)

--------------------------------------------------

*   Only works with C functions (not Luau closures)
*   Hooks execute on separate threads for better isolation
*   Use `oth.is_hook_thread()` to detect hook context
*   The returned original can be called to bypass the hook
*   Remove hooks with `oth.unhook`

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`oth.unhook`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/unhook)
     - Remove a hook
*   [`oth.get_root_callback`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback)
     - Get original function
*   [`oth.is_hook_thread`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread)
     - Check hook thread context

[oth.get\_root\_callback\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/get_root_callback)
[oth.is\_hook\_thread\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/is_hook_thread)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#example)
[Thread Safety](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#thread-safety)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#notes)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/oth/hook#related-functions)

[Input](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input)

mousemoverel
============

Moves the mouse cursor relative to its current position.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    mousemoverel(dx: number, dy: number) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `dx` | `number` | Horizontal offset in pixels |
| `dy` | `number` | Vertical offset in pixels |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`mousemoverel` moves the mouse cursor by the specified amount relative to its current position.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Move right 100 pixels
    mousemoverel(100, 0)
    
    -- Move down 50 pixels
    mousemoverel(0, 50)
    
    -- Move diagonally
    mousemoverel(50, 50)

[Circle Motion](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#circle-motion)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Draw a circle with mouse movement
    for i = 0, 360, 5 do
        local rad = math.rad(i)
        local dx = math.cos(rad) * 2
        local dy = math.sin(rad) * 2
        mousemoverel(dx, dy)
        task.wait(0.01)
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoverel#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`mousemoveabs`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousemoveabs)
     - Move to absolute position

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

writefile
=========

Writes data to a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    writefile(path: string, data: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path |
| `data` | `string` | The data to write |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`writefile` writes data to a file, creating the file if it doesn't exist or overwriting it if it does. Parent folders are created automatically.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Write a simple text file
    writefile("hello.txt", "Hello, World!")
    
    -- Verify the content
    print(readfile("hello.txt")) -- "Hello, World!"

[Writing JSON](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#writing-json)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    
    local settings = {
        volume = 0.5,
        graphics = "high",
        keybinds = {
            toggle = "F1",
            menu = "F2"
        }
    }
    
    writefile("settings.json", HttpService:JSONEncode(settings))

[Writing to Subfolders](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#writing-to-subfolders)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Parent folders are created automatically
    writefile("data/saves/slot1.txt", "Save data here")
    
    -- Or create them explicitly
    makefolder("logs")
    writefile("logs/session.log", "Session started")

[Binary Data](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#binary-data)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Write binary data (as string)
    local binary = string.char(0, 1, 2, 3, 255)
    writefile("binary.bin", binary)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
     - Read a file
*   [`appendfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile)
     - Append to a file
*   [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile)
     - Check if file exists

[readfile\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
[Input\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile#parameters)

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.generatekey
=================

Generates a random encryption key.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.generatekey() -> string

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | A Base64-encoded random key |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.generatekey` generates a cryptographically secure random key suitable for use with encryption functions.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Generate a key
    local key = crypt.generatekey()
    print("Generated key:", key)
    
    -- Use the key for encryption
    local data = "Secret message"
    local encrypted = crypt.encrypt(data, key)
    local decrypted = crypt.decrypt(encrypted, key)
    
    print("Original:", data)
    print("Decrypted:", decrypted)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   The key is suitable for AES encryption
*   Keys should be stored securely and not shared

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.encrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/encrypt)
     - Encrypt data
*   [`crypt.decrypt`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/decrypt)
     - Decrypt data
*   [`crypt.generatebytes`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes)
     - Generate raw bytes

getgamestate

    local gameState = getgamestate()

    print("Is Actor State:", gameState.IsActorState) -- false

    local gameState = getgamestate()

        print("Executed on game state!")\
    ]])

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local gameState = getgamestate()
    local currentState = getluastate()
    
    if gameState.Id == currentState.Id then
        print("Running on game state")
    else
        print("Running on different state")
    end

# Volt Documentation

[Environment](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

getgenv
=======

Returns the volt's global environment table.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    getgenv() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | The volt's global environment |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getgenv` returns the global environment table used by volt. Variables stored here persist across different script executions and can be accessed by all scripts running in volt.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Store a value in the volt environment
    getgenv().myGlobalValue = "Hello from script 1"
    
    -- Later, in another script execution
    print(getgenv().myGlobalValue) -- "Hello from script 1"

[Shared State](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#shared-state)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Script 1: Initialize shared state
    getgenv().SharedData = {
        players = {},
        settings = {
            enabled = true
        }
    }
    
    -- Script 2: Access shared state
    if getgenv().SharedData then
        print("Settings:", getgenv().SharedData.settings.enabled)
    end

[Checking if Script Already Ran](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#checking-if-script-already-ran)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    if getgenv().MyScriptLoaded then
        warn("Script already running!")
        return
    end
    getgenv().MyScriptLoaded = true
    
    -- Rest of your script...

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

     - Get game's environment
*   [`getsenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)
     - Get a script's environment

# Volt Documentation

[WebSocket](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

WebSocket.connect
=================

Creates a new WebSocket connection to the specified URL.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    WebSocket.connect(url: string) -> WebSocket

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `url` | `string` | The WebSocket URL to connect to |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `WebSocket` | A WebSocket object with methods and events |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`WebSocket.connect` establishes a persistent connection to a WebSocket server. The URL must use the `ws://` or `wss://` protocol (wss for secure/encrypted connections).

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Connect to a WebSocket server
    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.org")
    
    -- Handle incoming messages
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    -- Handle connection close
    ws.OnClose:Connect(function()
        print("Connection closed")
    end)
    
    -- Send a message
    ws:Send("Hello, WebSocket!")

[Echo Server Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#echo-server-example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.org")
    
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(msg)
        print("Echo:", msg)
    end)
    
    -- Send messages that will be echoed back
    ws:Send("Test message 1")
    ws:Send("Test message 2")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   WebSocket URLs must use `ws://` or `wss://` protocol
*   `wss://` is WebSocket Secure (encrypted)
*   Connection is maintained until closed or server disconnects

[Related](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#related)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`WebSocket:Send`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send)
     - Send messages
*   [`WebSocket:Close`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close)
     - Close connection
*   [`OnMessage`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage)
     - Receive messages

[WebSocket:Close\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close)
[WebSocket.OnClose\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#example)
[Echo Server Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect#echo-server-example)

# Volt Documentation

[VoltSignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

VoltConnection:Disconnect
=========================

Disconnects the connection from the signal.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    VoltConnection:Disconnect() -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This method does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`VoltConnection:Disconnect` removes the handler from the signal. After disconnecting, the handler will no longer be called when the signal fires.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    local connection = signal:Connect(function()
        print("This will only print once")
    end)
    
    signal:Fire()
    -- Output: This will only print once
    
    -- Disconnect the handler
    connection:Disconnect()
    
    signal:Fire()
    -- No output - handler is disconnected

[One-Time Connection Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#one-time-connection-pattern)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    local connection
    connection = signal:Connect(function(value)
        print("Received:", value)
        connection:Disconnect() -- Disconnect after first fire
    end)
    
    signal:Fire("First")  -- Output: Received: First
    signal:Fire("Second") -- No output

[Cleanup Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#cleanup-pattern)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    local connections = {}
    
    -- Store connections for cleanup
    table.insert(connections, signal:Connect(function()
        print("Handler 1")
    end))
    
    table.insert(connections, signal:Connect(function()
        print("Handler 2")
    end))
    
    -- Cleanup all connections
    for _, conn in ipairs(connections) do
        conn:Disconnect()
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`VoltSignal:Connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect)
     - Create a connection

[VoltSignal:Connect\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect)
[VoltSignal:Fire\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#example)
[One-Time Connection Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect#one-time-connection-pattern)

cansignalreplicate
==================

Checks if a signal can be replicated to the server.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    cansignalreplicate(signal: RBXScriptSignal) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate#parameters)

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the signal can replicate |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`cansignalreplicate` checks whether a given signal can be fired with server replication using `replicatesignal`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local prompt = workspace.Door.ProximityPrompt
    
    if cansignalreplicate(prompt.Triggered) then
        print("This signal can be replicated!")
        replicatesignal(prompt.Triggered, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
    else
        print("This signal cannot be replicated")
    end

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy:GetActors
=======================

Returns all Actor instances associated with this Lua state.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    state:GetActors() -> {Actor}

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{Actor}` | Array of Actor instances for this state |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy:GetActors` returns all Actor instances that are associated with this Lua state. For actor states, this will return the actors using that state. For the game state, this will return an empty array.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    local actors = state:GetActors()
    
    print("Actors in state:", #actors)
    for i, actor in ipairs(actors) do
        print(i, actor:GetFullName())
    end

[Actor State Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#actor-state-example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local actor = Instance.new("Actor")
    actor.Parent = workspace
    
    local actorState = getluastate(actor)
    local actors = actorState:GetActors()
    
    -- Should contain the actor we just created
    for _, a in ipairs(actors) do
        print("Actor:", a:GetFullName())
    end

[Filter by State](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#filter-by-state)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local allStates = getactorstates()
    
    for _, state in ipairs(allStates) do
        if state.IsActorState then
            local actors = state:GetActors()
            print("State", state.Id, "has", #actors, "actors")
        end
    end

[Related Methods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors#related-methods)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`LuaStateProxy:Execute`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute)
     - Execute code on the state
*   [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate)
     - Get state for an actor
