# Volt Documentation

[Environment](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

getreg
======

Returns the Lua registry table.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    getreg() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | The Lua registry |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getreg` returns the Lua registry, a special table used internally by Lua to store references. This can contain connections, threads, and other internal objects.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local registry = getreg()
    
    for i, v in pairs(registry) do
        print(i, type(v), v)
    end

[Finding Connections](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#finding-connections)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find all RBXScriptConnections in the registry
    local connections = {}
    for _, v in pairs(getreg()) do
        if type(v) == "table" then
            for _, item in pairs(v) do
                local t = typeof(item)
                if t == "RBXScriptConnection" then
                    table.insert(connections, item)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    print("Found", #connections, "connections")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   The registry contains internal Lua objects
*   Modifying the registry can cause undefined behavior
*   Use with caution and primarily for reading

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getgenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv)
     - Get volt's environment
*   [`getrenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv)
     - Get game environment

[getgenv\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv)
[getrenv\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.setupvalue
================

Sets an upvalue in a function by index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.setupvalue(func: function | number, index: number, value: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |
| `index` | `number` | The upvalue index (1-based) |
| `value` | `any` | The new value for the upvalue |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.setupvalue` modifies an upvalue (captured variable) in a function. Changes affect the shared variable, so all functions that capture the same upvalue will see the change.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    local count = 0
    
    local function getCount()
        return count
    end
    
    local function increment()
        count = count + 1
    end
    
    print(getCount()) -- 0
    
    -- Directly modify the upvalue
    debug.setupvalue(getCount, 1, 100)
    
    print(getCount()) -- 100
    increment()
    print(getCount()) -- 101

[Shared Upvalues](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#shared-upvalues)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When multiple functions share an upvalue, modifying it affects all of them:

    local shared = "original"
    
    local function read()
        return shared
    end
    
    local function write(val)
        shared = val
    end
    
    -- Both functions share the same upvalue
    debug.setupvalue(read, 1, "modified")
    
    print(read())  -- "modified"
    print(write)   -- The write function also sees the change

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue)
     - Get an upvalue
*   [`debug.getupvalues`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues)
     - Get all upvalues

[debug.setstack\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack)
[debug.validlevel\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#example)
[Shared Upvalues](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#shared-upvalues)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getsenv
=======

Gets a script's environment table.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    getsenv(script: LocalScript | ModuleScript) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `script` | `LocalScript` or `ModuleScript` | The script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | The script's environment |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

`getsenv` returns the environment table (`_ENV`) of a script, giving access to all its local and global variables.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    local scripts = getrunningscripts()
    if #scripts > 0 then
        local env = getsenv(scripts[1])
    
        print("Variables in script:")
        for key, value in pairs(env) do
            print("-", key, "=", type(value))
        end
    end

[Accessing Script Variables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#accessing-script-variables)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function getScriptVariable(scriptName, varName)
        for _, script in ipairs(getrunningscripts()) do
            if script.Name == scriptName then
                local env = getsenv(script)
                return env[varName]
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    
    local playerData = getScriptVariable("MainScript", "PlayerData")
    if playerData then
        print("Found player data!")
    end

[Modifying Script Variables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#modifying-script-variables)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local env = getsenv(targetScript)
    if env then
        -- Modify a variable
        env.SomeFlag = true
    
        -- Call a function from the script
        if env.SomeFunction then
            env.SomeFunction()
        end
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getgenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv)
     - Get volt's environment
*   [`getrenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv)
     - Get game environment

mousescroll
===========

Simulates mouse wheel scrolling.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousescroll#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    mousescroll(delta: number) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousescroll#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `delta` | `number` | Scroll amount (positive = up, negative = down) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousescroll#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousescroll#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`mousescroll` simulates scrolling the mouse wheel. Positive values scroll up, negative values scroll down.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mousescroll#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Scroll up
    mousescroll(3)
    
    -- Scroll down
    mousescroll(-3)
    
    -- Smooth scroll
    for i = 1, 10 do
        mousescroll(1)
        task.wait(0.05)
    end

# Volt Documentation

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

setclipboard
============

Copies text to the system clipboard.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    setclipboard(text: string) -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `toclipboard`
*   `setrbxclipboard`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `text` | `string` | The text to copy |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setclipboard` copies the provided text to the system clipboard, allowing it to be pasted elsewhere.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Copy a simple message
    setclipboard("Hello, World!")
    
    -- Copy player information
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    setclipboard(player.Name .. " - " .. player.UserId)
    
    -- Copy a table as JSON
    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    local data = {name = "Player", score = 100}
    setclipboard(HttpService:JSONEncode(data))

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Works with any string data
*   Useful for copying large amounts of data

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setclipboard#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`identifyexecutor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor)
     - Get executor info

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

appendfile
==========

Appends data to the end of a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    appendfile(path: string, data: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path |
| `data` | `string` | The data to append |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`appendfile` adds data to the end of an existing file without overwriting its contents. If the file doesn't exist, it will be created.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create initial file
    writefile("log.txt", "Log started\n")
    
    -- Append entries
    appendfile("log.txt", "Entry 1: Hello\n")
    appendfile("log.txt", "Entry 2: World\n")
    
    -- Read the result
    print(readfile("log.txt"))
    --[[\
    Log started\
    Entry 1: Hello\
    Entry 2: World\
    ]]

[Logging Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#logging-example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function log(message)
        local timestamp = os.date("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        appendfile("debug.log", "[" .. timestamp .. "] " .. message .. "\n")
    end
    
    log("Script started")
    log("Player joined")
    log("Event triggered")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`writefile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/writefile)
     - Overwrite a file
*   [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
     - Read a file

[Filesystem\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)
[delfile\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile)

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

getluastate
===========

Returns the LuaStateProxy for a given Actor or loaded script.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    getluastate(actor_or_script: (Actor | BaseScript)?) -> LuaStateProxy

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `actor_or_script` | `Actor \| BaseScript?` | The Actor or script to get the state for. If omitted, returns current state |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `LuaStateProxy` | The LuaStateProxy for the given Actor or script, or current state |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getluastate` returns the `LuaStateProxy` object for a specific Actor or loaded script. If no argument is provided, it returns the `LuaStateProxy` for the current Lua state.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get current state
    local currentState = getluastate()
    print("Current state ID:", currentState.Id)
    
    -- Get state for an actor
    local actor = Instance.new("Actor")
    actor.Parent = workspace
    local actorState = getluastate(actor)
    print("Actor state ID:", actorState.Id, "Is Actor:", actorState.IsActorState)

[Get State for Script](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#get-state-for-script)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get state for a specific script
    local script = workspace.SomeScript
    local scriptState = getluastate(script)
    print("Script state ID:", scriptState.Id)

[Access State Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#access-state-properties)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    print("State ID:", state.Id)
    print("Is Actor State:", state.IsActorState)
    
    -- Get all actors for this state
    local actors = state:GetActors()
    print("Actors in state:", #actors)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getactorstates`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates)
     - Get all active LuaStateProxy objects
*   [`getgamestate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getgamestate)
     - Get the default game Lua state
*   [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors)
     - Get all Actor instances

\

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel)

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy.Id
================

Unique identifier for this Lua state.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    state.Id: number

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy.Id` is a read-only property that returns a unique numeric identifier for the Lua state. Each state (game state and actor states) has its own unique ID.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    print("State ID:", state.Id)

[Compare States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#compare-states)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local gameState = getgamestate()
    local currentState = getluastate()
    
    if gameState.Id == currentState.Id then
        print("Running on game state")
    else
        print("Running on different state (ID:", currentState.Id, ")")
    end

[Track States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#track-states)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local states = getactorstates()
    local stateIds = {}
    
    for _, state in ipairs(states) do
        table.insert(stateIds, state.Id)
        print("State ID:", state.Id, "Is Actor:", state.IsActorState)
    end

[Related Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id#related-properties)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`LuaStateProxy.IsActorState`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate)
     - Check if state is for actors
*   [`LuaStateProxy.Event`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/event)
     - Communication event

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

setfflag
========

Sets a Roblox Fast Flag value.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    setfflag(name: string, value: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `name` | `string` | The flag name |
| `value` | `string` | The value to set |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setfflag` sets the value of a Roblox Fast Flag (FFlag). These flags control various engine features and behaviors.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Enable a flag
    setfflag("DFIntTaskSchedulerTargetFps", "240")
    
    -- Disable graphics features
    setfflag("FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryEphemeralCounter", "true")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Flag names are case-sensitive
*   Values are always strings
*   Some flags require restart to take effect
*   Not all flags can be modified

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfflag#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getfflag`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/getfflag)
     - Get flag value

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

cloneref
========

Creates a new reference to an instance that compares as different.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    cloneref(instance: Instance) -> Instance

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to clone a reference to |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Instance` | A new reference to the same instance |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`cloneref` creates a new reference to an instance. The cloned reference points to the same underlying object, but the two references are not equal when compared with `==`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    local clone = cloneref(part)
    
    -- Both reference the same instance
    print(part.Name)  -- "Part"
    print(clone.Name) -- "Part"
    
    -- But they compare as different
    print(part == clone) -- false
    
    -- Changes through one affect the other
    clone.Name = "Renamed"
    print(part.Name) -- "Renamed"

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#use-cases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Anti-detection**: Prevent games from detecting your references
*   **Reference hiding**: Create references that can't be found through equality checks

[Verification](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#verification)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Verify they're the same underlying instance
    print(compareinstances(part, clone)) -- true

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`compareinstances`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances)
     - Compare two references

[Instances\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)
[compareinstances\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#example)
[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref#use-cases)

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.hash
==========

Generates a hash of the provided data.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.hash(data: string, algorithm: string?) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The data to hash |
| `algorithm` | `string` | (Optional) Hash algorithm, default "SHA256" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The hexadecimal hash string |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.hash` generates a cryptographic hash of the input data using the specified algorithm.

[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#supported-algorithms)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `MD5`
*   `SHA1`
*   `SHA256` (default)
*   `SHA384`
*   `SHA512`

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#example)

--------------------------------------------------------

    local data = "Hello, World!"
    
    -- Default SHA256
    local hash = crypt.hash(data)
    print("SHA256:", hash)
    
    -- Other algorithms
    print("MD5:", crypt.hash(data, "MD5"))
    print("SHA1:", crypt.hash(data, "SHA1"))
    print("SHA512:", crypt.hash(data, "SHA512"))

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#use-cases)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   Verifying data integrity
*   Creating unique identifiers
*   Password hashing (prefer `crypt.hmac` for security)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.hmac`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac)
     - HMAC authentication

[crypt.generatekey\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey)
[crypt.hmac\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#description)
[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#supported-algorithms)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash#example)

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

getrawmetatable
===============

Gets the raw metatable of an object, bypassing `__metatable`.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    getrawmetatable(object: any) -> table?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `object` | `any` | The object to get the metatable from |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table?` | The raw metatable, or nil if none |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getrawmetatable` retrieves the actual metatable of an object, bypassing the `__metatable` field that would normally prevent access via `getmetatable`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Normal getmetatable is blocked on Roblox objects
    print(getmetatable(game)) -- "The metatable is locked"
    
    -- getrawmetatable bypasses this
    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    print(mt) -- table: 0x...
    print(mt.__index) -- function
    print(mt.__namecall) -- function

[Inspecting Metamethods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#inspecting-metamethods)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    for key, value in pairs(mt) do
        print(key, type(value))
    end
    --[[\
    __index      function\
    __newindex   function\
    __namecall   function\
    __tostring   function\
    ...\
    ]]

[Before Hooking](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#before-hooking)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Always get the metatable before modifying
    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    local oldIndex = mt.__index
    
    -- You may need to unlock it first
    setreadonly(mt, false)
    mt.__index = newcclosure(function(self, key)
        print("Indexing:", key)
        return oldIndex(self, key)
    end)
    setreadonly(mt, true)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`setrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable)
     - Set a raw metatable
*   [`setreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly)
     - Unlock the metatable

[getnamecallmethod\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod)
[isreadonly\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#example)
[Inspecting Metamethods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable#inspecting-metamethods)

# Volt Documentation

[Signals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

firesignal
==========

Fires a signal with the given arguments.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    firesignal(signal: RBXScriptSignal, ...: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `signal` | `RBXScriptSignal` | The signal to fire |
| `...` | `any` | Arguments to pass to handlers |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`firesignal` triggers all connected handlers of a signal with the provided arguments. This simulates the signal being fired naturally.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Fire a button's MouseButton1Click
    local button = PlayerGui.ScreenGui.TextButton
    firesignal(button.MouseButton1Click)
    
    -- Fire with arguments
    firesignal(someObject.CustomEvent, "arg1", 123, true)

[Firing Input Events](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#firing-input-events)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Simulate a key press
    local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
    
    local inputObject = Instance.new("InputObject") -- Pseudocode
    firesignal(UserInputService.InputBegan, inputObject, false)

[Firing Touch Events](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#firing-touch-events)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.TouchPart
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    local hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
    
    -- Fire the Touched event
    firesignal(part.Touched, hrp)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   All connected handlers will be called
*   Arguments are passed to each handler
*   Use `getconnections` to fire specific connections only

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getconnections`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections)
     - Get signal connections
*   [`replicatesignal`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal)
     - Fire with replication

[cansignalreplicate\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate)
[getconnections\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal#example)

gethiddenproperties
===================

Gets all hidden properties of an instance.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    gethiddenproperties(instance: Instance) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Dictionary of hidden property values |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`gethiddenproperties` returns a table containing all hidden (non-scriptable) properties and their current values.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    local hidden = gethiddenproperties(part)
    
    for property, value in pairs(hidden) do
        print(property, "=", value)
    end

# Volt Documentation

[Environment](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment)

getrenv
=======

Returns the game's global environment table.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    getrenv() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | The game's global environment |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getrenv` returns the global environment used by game scripts. This contains all standard Roblox globals like `game`, `workspace`, `Instance`, etc.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    local renv = getrenv()
    
    -- Access game globals
    print(renv.game)      -- Same as game
    print(renv.workspace) -- Same as workspace
    print(renv.Instance)  -- Same as Instance

[Finding Game Globals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#finding-game-globals)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- List all globals in the game environment
    local renv = getrenv()
    for name, value in pairs(renv) do
        print(name, type(value))
    end

[Difference from getgenv](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#difference-from-getgenv)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| `getrenv()` | `getgenv()` |
| --- | --- |
| Game's environment | Volt's environment |
| Contains Roblox globals | Contains volt globals |
| Read-only access recommended | Can freely modify |

[Checking for Global Modifications](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#checking-for-global-modifications)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Check if game modified a global
    local renv = getrenv()
    if renv.print ~= print then
        warn("print function was modified!")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getrenv#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getgenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getgenv)
     - Get volt's environment
*   [`getsenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)
     - Get a script's environment

Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/getreg)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv)

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.hmac
==========

Generates an HMAC (Hash-based Message Authentication Code).

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.hmac(data: string, key: string, algorithm: string?) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `data` | `string` | The data to authenticate |
| `key` | `string` | The secret key |
| `algorithm` | `string` | (Optional) Hash algorithm, default "SHA256" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The HMAC as a hex string |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.hmac` generates a keyed-hash message authentication code, which provides both data integrity and authentication.

[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#supported-algorithms)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `MD5`
*   `SHA1`
*   `SHA256` (default)
*   `SHA384`
*   `SHA512`

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#example)

--------------------------------------------------------

    local data = "Important message"
    local key = "secret_key"
    
    local mac = crypt.hmac(data, key, "SHA256")
    print("HMAC:", mac)

[Verification Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#verification-example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function verifyMessage(data, key, expectedHmac)
        local computed = crypt.hmac(data, key)
        return computed == expectedHmac
    end
    
    local key = "my_secret"
    local message = "Hello"
    local signature = crypt.hmac(message, key)
    
    -- Later, verify the message
    if verifyMessage(message, key, signature) then
        print("Message is authentic!")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.hash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash)
     - Simple hashing

[crypt.hash\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hash)
[crypt.random\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#description)
[Supported Algorithms](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac#supported-algorithms)

# Volt Documentation

[WebSocket](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

WebSocket.OnClose
=================

Signal that fires when the WebSocket connection is closed.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    WebSocket.OnClose:Connect(callback: () -> ()) -> Connection

[Callback Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#callback-parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This callback receives no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Connection` | A connection that can be disconnected |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`OnClose` is a signal that fires when the WebSocket connection is terminated, either by calling `Close()` or when the server disconnects.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    
    ws.OnClose:Connect(function()
        print("Connection closed")
    end)
    
    -- Later...
    ws:Close()
    -- Output: Connection closed

[Reconnection Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#reconnection-pattern)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function createConnection()
        local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
        
        ws.OnClose:Connect(function()
            print("Disconnected, reconnecting in 5 seconds...")
            task.wait(5)
            createConnection()
        end)
        
        ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(msg)
            print("Message:", msg)
        end)
        
        return ws
    end
    
    local connection = createConnection()

[Cleanup on Close](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#cleanup-on-close)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    local isConnected = true
    
    ws.OnClose:Connect(function()
        isConnected = false
        print("Cleaning up...")
        -- Perform cleanup tasks
    end)
    
    -- Check connection state before sending
    if isConnected then
        ws:Send("Hello!")
    end

[Related](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#related)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`WebSocket.connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)
     - Create connection
*   [`WebSocket:Close`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/close)
     - Close connection
*   [`OnMessage`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage)
     - Message event

[WebSocket.connect\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)
[WebSocket.OnMessage\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#syntax)
[Callback Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#callback-parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onclose#description)

# Volt Documentation

[VoltSignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

VoltSignal:Fire
===============

Fires the signal with the given arguments.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    VoltSignal:Fire(...: any) -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `...` | `any` | Arguments to pass to connected handlers |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------

This method does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

`VoltSignal:Fire` triggers all connected handlers and resumes any threads waiting on the signal. All provided arguments are passed to each handler and returned by `Wait`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    signal:Connect(function(a, b, c)
        print(a, b, c)
    end)
    
    -- Fire with multiple arguments
    signal:Fire("hello", 42, true)
    -- Output: hello 42 true

[Firing Without Arguments](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#firing-without-arguments)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local onComplete = VoltSignal.new()
    
    onComplete:Connect(function()
        print("Task completed!")
    end)
    
    onComplete:Fire()
    -- Output: Task completed!

[Firing With Tables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#firing-with-tables)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local onDataReceived = VoltSignal.new()
    
    onDataReceived:Connect(function(data)
        print("Received:", data.name, data.value)
    end)
    
    onDataReceived:Fire({ name = "Score", value = 100 })
    -- Output: Received: Score 100

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`VoltSignal:Connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect)
     - Connect handlers
*   [`VoltSignal:Wait`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait)
     - Wait for fire

[VoltConnection:Disconnect\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/disconnect)
[VoltSignal.new\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Input](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input)

iswindowactive
==============

Checks if the game window is currently focused.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    iswindowactive() -> boolean

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `isrbxactive`
*   `isgameactive`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if game window is focused |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`iswindowactive` returns whether the Roblox game window is currently the active/focused window. This is useful for input simulation to ensure inputs only occur when the game is focused.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Only simulate input when game is focused
    if iswindowactive() then
        keypress(0x20) -- Press space
        task.wait(0.1)
        keyrelease(0x20)
    end

[Wait for Focus](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#wait-for-focus)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Wait until game is focused before executing
    repeat task.wait() until iswindowactive()
    print("Game is now focused!")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/iswindowactive#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`keypress`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress)
     - Simulate key press
*   [`mouse1click`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1click)
     - Simulate mouse click

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keyclick)

rconsolehidden
==============

Checks if the console window is hidden.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehidden#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsolehidden() -> boolean

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehidden#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if console is hidden/closed |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehidden#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsolehidden` returns whether the console window is currently hidden or not visible.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehidden#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleshow()
    
    if not rconsolehidden() then
        rconsoleprint("Console is visible!\n")
    end
    
    rconsolehide()
    
    if rconsolehidden() then
        print("Console is now hidden")
    end

     - Hide the console

# Volt Documentation

[VoltSignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

VoltSignal.new
==============

Creates a new VoltSignal instance.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    VoltSignal.new() -> VoltSignal

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

This function takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `VoltSignal` | A new VoltSignal instance |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`VoltSignal.new` creates a new signal object that can be used to implement custom events. The returned signal can have handlers connected to it and can be fired with arguments.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a new signal
    local onPlayerDamaged = VoltSignal.new()
    
    -- Connect a handler
    onPlayerDamaged:Connect(function(player, damage)
        print(player.Name .. " took " .. damage .. " damage!")
    end)
    
    -- Fire the signal
    onPlayerDamaged:Fire(game.Players.LocalPlayer, 50)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`VoltSignal:Connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect)
     - Connect a handler
*   [`VoltSignal:Fire`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire)
     - Fire the signal

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire)

\

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

setstackhidden
==============

Sets whether a function is hidden from stack traces.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    setstackhidden(func: function, hidden: boolean) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to modify |
| `hidden` | `boolean` | Whether to hide from stack |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setstackhidden` controls whether a function appears in stack traces and debug info. Hidden functions are invisible to stack inspection.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function secretFunc()
        print("This function is hidden!")
    end
    
    setstackhidden(secretFunc, true)
    
    -- Now secretFunc won't appear in debug.traceback()

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#use-cases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Hiding hook implementations
*   Preventing detection via stack inspection
*   Clean stack traces

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/setstackhidden#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getinfo`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo)
     - Get function info
*   [`debug.getcallstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack)
     - Get call stack

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

delfile
=======

Deletes a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    delfile(path: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path to delete |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`delfile` permanently deletes a file at the specified path.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a file
    writefile("temp.txt", "Temporary data")
    
    -- Verify it exists
    print(isfile("temp.txt")) -- true
    
    -- Delete it
    delfile("temp.txt")
    
    -- Verify it's gone
    print(isfile("temp.txt")) -- false

[Safe Delete](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#safe-delete)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeDelete(path)
        if isfile(path) then
            delfile(path)
            return true
        end
        return false
    end
    
    if safeDelete("myfile.txt") then
        print("File deleted")
    else
        print("File didn't exist")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile)
     - Check if file exists
*   [`delfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder)
     - Delete a folder

Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/appendfile)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

compareinstances
================

Compares if two references point to the same instance.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    compareinstances(a: Instance, b: Instance) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `a` | `Instance` | First instance reference |
| `b` | `Instance` | Second instance reference |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if both point to the same instance |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`compareinstances` checks if two instance references point to the same underlying Roblox instance, even if they were created with `cloneref`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    local clone = cloneref(part)
    local other = workspace.OtherPart
    
    -- Normal comparison fails for cloneref
    print(part == clone) -- false
    
    -- compareinstances works correctly
    print(compareinstances(part, clone)) -- true
    print(compareinstances(part, other)) -- false

[Use Case](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#use-case)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function findInTable(tbl, target)
        for _, item in ipairs(tbl) do
            if typeof(item) == "Instance" and compareinstances(item, target) then
                return true
            end
        end
        return false
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`cloneref`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref)
     - Clone an instance reference

[cloneref\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/cloneref)
[fireclickdetector\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/compareinstances#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

isparallel
==========

Checks if the current thread is running in parallel.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    isparallel() -> boolean

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#aliases)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   `is_parallel`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if running in a parallel context |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`isparallel` returns whether the current code is executing in a parallel Luau context (inside an Actor).

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    if isparallel() then
        print("Running in parallel!")
        -- Safe to do parallel-safe operations
    else
        print("Running on main thread")
    end

[Use in Actor](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#use-in-actor)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    run_on_actor(someActor, [[\
        print("Is parallel:", isparallel()) -- true\
    ]])
    
    print("Is parallel:", isparallel()) -- false (main thread)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns `false` on the main game thread
*   Returns `true` when running inside an actor via `run_on_actor`

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`run_on_actor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor)
     - Run code on an actor
*   [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors)
     - Get all actors

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy.IsActorState
==========================

Whether this state was created for use by Actors.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    state.IsActorState: boolean

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy.IsActorState` is a read-only boolean property that indicates whether the Lua state was created for use by Actors. Returns `true` for actor states and `false` for the main game state.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    if state.IsActorState then
        print("This is an actor state")
    else
        print("This is the game state")
    end

[Filter Actor States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#filter-actor-states)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local states = getactorstates()
    local actorStates = {}
    
    for _, state in ipairs(states) do
        if state.IsActorState then
            table.insert(actorStates, state)
            print("Actor state ID:", state.Id)
        end
    end
    
    print("Total actor states:", #actorStates)

[Conditional Behavior](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#conditional-behavior)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = getluastate()
    
    if state.IsActorState then
        -- Actor-specific logic
        print("Running on actor state")
        local actors = state:GetActors()
        print("Actors in state:", #actors)
    else
        -- Game state logic
        print("Running on game state")
    end

[Related Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/isactorstate#related-properties)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`LuaStateProxy.Id`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/id)
     - Unique state identifier
*   [`LuaStateProxy:GetActors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/getactors)
     - Get actors for this state

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

hookfunction
============

Replaces a function with a custom implementation.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    hookfunction(target: function, hook: function) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `target` | `function` | The function to hook |
| `hook` | `function` | The replacement function |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A reference to the original function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`hookfunction` replaces the target function with your hook function. All calls to the original function will now go through your hook instead. The function returns a reference to the original, allowing you to call it from within your hook.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook the print function
    local originalPrint = hookfunction(print, function(...)
        originalPrint("[PREFIX]", ...)
    end)
    
    print("Hello") -- Output: [PREFIX] Hello
    
    -- You can still use the original
    originalPrint("Direct call") -- Output: Direct call

[Advanced Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#advanced-example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook a game method
    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookfunction(
        getrawmetatable(game).__namecall,
        newcclosure(function(self, ...)
            local method = getnamecallmethod()
    
            if method == "Kick" then
                return -- Block kick
            end
    
            return oldNamecall(self, ...)
        end)
    )

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use `checkcaller` to differentiate between your calls and game calls
*   Automatically wrapps Luau hooks in `newcclosure` when hooking C closures
*   The returned original can be called to bypass the hook
*   Restore the hook with `restorefunction`

[getfunctionhash\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash)
[hookmetamethod\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#example)
[Advanced Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction#advanced-example)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getconstant
=================

Gets a constant from a function at the specified index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getconstant(func: function | number, index: number) -> any

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |
| `index` | `number` | The constant index (1-based) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The constant value at the specified index |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getconstant` retrieves a constant value from a function's bytecode. Constants are literal values like strings, numbers, and booleans that are embedded in the compiled function.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    local function example()
        local x = "hello"
        local y = 42
        print(x, y)
    end
    
    -- Get constants from the function
    print(debug.getconstant(example, 1)) -- "hello"
    print(debug.getconstant(example, 2)) -- 42
    print(debug.getconstant(example, 3)) -- "print" (function name)

[Using Stack Level](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#using-stack-level)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also pass a stack level instead of a function:

    local function inner()
        -- Get constant from the calling function (level 2)
        print(debug.getconstant(2, 1))
    end
    
    local function outer()
        local msg = "from outer"
        inner()
    end
    
    outer() -- Prints a constant from outer

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   Index is 1-based
*   Not all indices may have constants (some may be nil)
*   Only works with Luau closures

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getconstants`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants)
     - Get all constants
*   [`debug.setconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant)
     - Modify a constant

[debug.getcallstack\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack)
[debug.getconstants\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#example)
[Using Stack Level](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant#using-stack-level)

# Volt Documentation

[VoltSignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal)

VoltSignal:Wait
===============

Yields the current thread until the signal fires.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    VoltSignal:Wait() -> any

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This method takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The arguments passed to `Fire` |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

`VoltSignal:Wait` pauses the current thread until the signal is fired. When the signal fires, the thread resumes and returns any arguments that were passed to `Fire`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    -- In another thread, fire after 2 seconds
    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(2)
        signal:Fire("Data loaded!", 100)
    end)
    
    -- Wait for the signal
    local message, value = signal:Wait()
    print(message, value)
    -- Output (after 2 seconds): Data loaded! 100

[Timeout Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#timeout-pattern)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local signal = VoltSignal.new()
    
    local result
    local timedOut = false
    
    task.spawn(function()
        result = signal:Wait()
    end)
    
    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(5)
        if not result then
            timedOut = true
            -- Handle timeout
        end
    end)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`VoltSignal:Fire`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/fire)
     - Fire the signal
*   [`VoltSignal:Connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/connect)
     - Connect without yielding

[VoltSignal.new\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/new)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/voltsignal/wait#example)

# Volt Documentation

[WebSocket](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

WebSocket.OnMessage
===================

Signal that fires when a message is received from the server.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    WebSocket.OnMessage:Connect(callback: (message: string) -> ()) -> Connection

[Callback Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#callback-parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `message` | `string` | The received message |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Connection` | A connection that can be disconnected |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`OnMessage` is a signal that fires whenever the WebSocket server sends a message. Connect a handler function to process incoming messages.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.org")
    
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    ws:Send("Hello!")
    -- Output: Received: Hello!

[JSON Messages](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#json-messages)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://api.example.com/ws")
    
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(message)
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(message)
        
        if data.type == "update" then
            print("Update:", data.payload)
        elseif data.type == "error" then
            warn("Error:", data.message)
        end
    end)

[Message Queue Pattern](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#message-queue-pattern)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    local messageQueue = {}
    
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(message)
        table.insert(messageQueue, {
            content = message,
            time = os.time()
        })
    end)
    
    -- Process messages elsewhere
    local function processQueue()
        for _, msg in ipairs(messageQueue) do
            print(msg.time, msg.content)
        end
        table.clear(messageQueue)
    end

[Related](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage#related)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`WebSocket.connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)
     - Create connection

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

isreadonly
==========

Checks if a table is read-only.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    isreadonly(table: table) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `table` | `table` | The table to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the table is read-only |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isreadonly` returns whether a table has been marked as read-only, preventing modifications.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    print(isreadonly(mt)) -- true (Roblox metatables are locked)
    
    -- Normal tables are not read-only by default
    local myTable = {a = 1}
    print(isreadonly(myTable)) -- false

[Before Modifying](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#before-modifying)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    if isreadonly(mt) then
        setreadonly(mt, false)
        -- Now safe to modify
        mt.__index = myCustomIndex
        setreadonly(mt, true)
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`setreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly)
     - Set read-only status
*   [`getrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable)
     - Get the metatable

[getrawmetatable\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable)
[iswritable\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable)

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly#description)
