gettenv
=======

Gets the environment of a thread.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    gettenv(thread: thread?) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `thread` | `thread` | (Optional) Thread, defaults to current |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | The thread's environment |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`gettenv` returns the environment table for the specified thread. If no thread is provided, returns the current thread's environment.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/environment/gettenv#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get current thread's environment
    local env = gettenv()
    print(env.print) -- The print function
    
    -- Get another thread's environment
    local thread = coroutine.create(function() end)
    local threadEnv = gettenv(thread)

# Volt Documentation

[Signals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

getconnections
==============

Gets all connections to a signal.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    getconnections(signal: RBXScriptSignal) -> {Connection}

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `signal` | `RBXScriptSignal` | The signal |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{Connection}` | Array of Connection objects |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getconnections` returns all current connections to a signal, allowing you to inspect, fire, disable, or disconnect them individually.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local connections = getconnections(game.Players.PlayerAdded)
    
    print("Total connections:", #connections)
    
    for i, conn in ipairs(connections) do
        print(i, "Enabled:", conn.Enabled)
    end

[Disconnecting All](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#disconnecting-all)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function disconnectAll(signal)
        for _, conn in ipairs(getconnections(signal)) do
            conn:Disconnect()
        end
    end
    
    -- Disconnect all PlayerAdded handlers
    disconnectAll(game.Players.PlayerAdded)

[Disabling Specific Connections](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#disabling-specific-connections)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local connections = getconnections(workspace.Part.Touched)
    
    for _, conn in ipairs(connections) do
        if conn.Function then
            -- Check if it's the function we want to disable
            conn:Disable()
        end
    end

[Inspecting Connection Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#inspecting-connection-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local connections = getconnections(someEvent)
    
    for _, conn in ipairs(connections) do
        if conn.LuaConnection and conn.Function then
            print("Found Lua connection")
            local constants = debug.getconstants(conn.Function)
            print("Constants:", table.concat(constants, ", "))
        end
    end

[The Connection Object](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#the-connection-object)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each connection returned has the following properties and methods:

| Property/Method | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Enabled` | `boolean` | Whether the connection is active |
| `ForeignState` | `boolean` | Whether it's from a different Luau state |
| `LuaConnection` | `boolean` | Whether it's a Lua connection |
| `Function` | `function` | The connected function (if accessible) |
| `Thread` | `thread` | The connection's thread |
| `Fire(...)` | `method` | Fire this connection only |
| `Defer(...)` | `method` | Deferred fire |
| `Disconnect()` | `method` | Disconnect this connection |
| `Disable()` | `method` | Temporarily disable |
| `Enable()` | `method` | Re-enable after disable |

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`firesignal`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal)
     - Fire all connections

[firesignal\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal)
[getsignalarguments\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalarguments)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getconnections#example)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

fireclickdetector
=================

Triggers a ClickDetector as if it was clicked.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    fireclickdetector(detector: ClickDetector, distance?: number, event?: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `detector` | `ClickDetector` | The ClickDetector to fire |
| `distance` | `number?` | The simulated click distance (default: 0) |
| `event` | `string?` | Event type: "MouseClick", "RightMouseClick", or "MouseHoverEnter/Leave" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`fireclickdetector` simulates a click on a ClickDetector, triggering its events without needing to be in range or actually clicking.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find a ClickDetector
    local detector = workspace.Button.ClickDetector
    
    -- Fire it
    fireclickdetector(detector)
    
    -- Fire with distance
    fireclickdetector(detector, 10)
    
    -- Fire right click
    fireclickdetector(detector, 0, "RightMouseClick")

[Finding and Clicking All](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#finding-and-clicking-all)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Click all ClickDetectors in a model
    local function clickAll(parent)
        for _, desc in ipairs(parent:GetDescendants()) do
            if desc:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                fireclickdetector(desc)
            end
        end
    end
    
    clickAll(workspace.Shop)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Distance is used for MaxActivationDistance checks in some games
*   Events: "MouseClick" (default), "RightMouseClick", "MouseHoverEnter", "MouseHoverLeave"

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt)

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getcallingscript
================

Returns the script that called the current function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    getcallingscript() -> LocalScript | ModuleScript | nil

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `LocalScript` or `ModuleScript` or `nil` | The calling script |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getcallingscript` returns a reference to the script that invoked the current function. This is useful in hooks to identify which script triggered the call.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local oldPrint = print
    print = function(...)
        local caller = getcallingscript()
        if caller then
            oldPrint("[" .. caller.Name .. "]", ...)
        else
            oldPrint("[Unknown]", ...)
        end
    end
    
    -- When a game script calls print, it shows which script

[In Metamethod Hooks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#in-metamethod-hooks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local caller = getcallingscript()
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
    
        if caller then
            print("Script:", caller:GetFullName())
            print("Method:", method)
        end
    
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns nil if called from volt (not from a game script)
*   Useful for filtering hooks based on the calling script
*   Works in hooked functions and metamethods

[Scripts\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)
[getloadedmodules\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#example)
[In Metamethod Hooks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript#in-metamethod-hooks)

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

gethiddenproperty
=================

Gets the value of a hidden property.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    gethiddenproperty(instance: Instance, property: string) -> any, boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance |
| `property` | `string` | The hidden property name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The property value |
| `boolean` | Whether the property was hidden |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`gethiddenproperty` retrieves the value of a property that isn't normally accessible through scripts.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = Instance.new("Part")
    
    -- Get a hidden property
    local value, wasHidden = gethiddenproperty(part, "size_xml")
    print("Value:", value)
    print("Was hidden:", wasHidden)

[Common Hidden Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#common-hidden-properties)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Class | Property | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `LocalScript` | `Bytecode` | Compiled bytecode |
| `Sound` | `RollOffMode` | Sound falloff mode |
| `Humanoid` | `InternalHeadScale` | Internal head scaling |

[Finding Hidden Properties](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#finding-hidden-properties)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Example of reading protected properties
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local character = player.Character
    
    if character then
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        if humanoid then
            local internal = gethiddenproperty(humanoid, "InternalHeadScale")
            print("Internal head scale:", internal)
        end
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`sethiddenproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/sethiddenproperty)
     - Set a hidden property
*   [`isscriptable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable)
     - Check if property is scriptable

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

iswritable
==========

Checks if a table is writable (not read-only).

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    iswritable(table: table) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `table` | `table` | The table to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the table can be modified |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`iswritable` checks whether a table can be modified. This is the inverse of `isreadonly` - it returns `true` when `isreadonly` would return `false`, and vice versa.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local myTable = {value = 123}
    
    print(iswritable(myTable)) -- true
    
    makereadonly(myTable)
    print(iswritable(myTable)) -- false
    
    makewritable(myTable)
    print(iswritable(myTable)) -- true

[Metatable Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#metatable-example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    if iswritable(mt) then
        print("Metatable is writable")
    else
        print("Metatable is read-only")
        makewritable(mt)
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   Equivalent to `not isreadonly(table)`
*   Useful for checking before modifications

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)
     - Check if table is read-only
*   [`makewritable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable)
     - Make table writable
*   [`makereadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly)
     - Make table read-only

[isreadonly\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)
[makereadonly\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#example)
[Metatable Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#metatable-example)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable#notes)

# Volt Documentation

[WebSocket](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket)

WebSocket:Send
==============

Sends a message through the WebSocket connection.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    WebSocket:Send(message: string) -> ()

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `message` | `string` | The message to send |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

This method does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`WebSocket:Send` transmits a string message to the connected WebSocket server. For structured data, encode it as JSON before sending.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://example.com/socket")
    
    -- Send a simple message
    ws:Send("Hello, Server!")

[JSON Communication](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#json-communication)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://api.example.com/ws")
    
    -- Send JSON data
    local function sendJSON(data)
        ws:Send(HttpService:JSONEncode(data))
    end
    
    sendJSON({
        type = "subscribe",
        channel = "updates"
    })
    
    sendJSON({
        type = "message",
        content = "Hello!",
        timestamp = os.time()
    })

[Multiple Messages](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#multiple-messages)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.org")
    
    ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(msg)
        print("Echo:", msg)
    end)
    
    -- Send multiple messages
    ws:Send("First message")
    ws:Send("Second message")
    ws:Send("Third message")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------

*   Messages are strings; use JSON for structured data
*   Messages are sent asynchronously
*   Connection must be open to send

[Related](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/send#related)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`WebSocket.connect`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/connect)
     - Create connection
*   [`OnMessage`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/websocket/onmessage)
     - Receive responses

[WebSocket.OnMessage\
\

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

clearqueueonteleport
====================

Clears the teleport script queue.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    clearqueueonteleport() -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#aliases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `clearteleportqueue`
*   `clear_teleport_queue`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`clearqueueonteleport` removes any script that was queued to run after teleporting.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Queue a script
    queueonteleport("print('Hello after teleport')")
    
    -- Change our mind
    clearqueueonteleport()
    
    -- Now nothing will run after teleporting

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`queueonteleport`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport)
     - Queue a teleport script

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getconstants
==================

Gets all constants from a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getconstants(func: function | number) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | An array of all constants in the function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getconstants` returns a table containing all constant values embedded in a function's bytecode. This is useful for inspecting what literal values a function uses.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local function greet(name)
        local greeting = "Hello"
        local punctuation = "!"
        return greeting .. ", " .. name .. punctuation
    end
    
    local constants = debug.getconstants(greet)
    for i, v in ipairs(constants) do
        print(i, type(v), v)
    end
    --[[\
    Output:\
    1  string  Hello\
    2  string  !\
    3  string  , \
    ]]

[Inspecting Game Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#inspecting-game-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find what strings a function uses
    local function findStrings(func)
        local strings = {}
        for i, const in ipairs(debug.getconstants(func)) do
            if type(const) == "string" then
                table.insert(strings, const)
            end
        end
        return strings
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   The table is indexed starting at 1
*   Some indices may contain `nil` for unused constant slots
*   Only works with Luau closures

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant)
     - Get a single constant
*   [`debug.setconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant)
     - Modify a constant

[debug.getconstant\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant)
[debug.getinfo\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

delfolder
=========

Deletes a folder and its contents.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    delfolder(path: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The folder path to delete |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`delfolder` permanently deletes a folder and all of its contents, including files and subfolders.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a folder structure
    makefolder("testfolder")
    writefile("testfolder/file1.txt", "Data 1")
    writefile("testfolder/file2.txt", "Data 2")
    
    -- Verify it exists
    print(isfolder("testfolder")) -- true
    
    -- Delete the entire folder
    delfolder("testfolder")
    
    -- Verify it's gone
    print(isfolder("testfolder")) -- false

This operation is irreversible. All files and subfolders will be permanently deleted.

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder)
     - Check if folder exists
*   [`delfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile)
     - Delete a single file
*   [`makefolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder)
     - Create a folder

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfile)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

on\_actor\_added
================

A bindable event that fires when an actor is added and ready.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_added: BindableEvent

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`on_actor_added` is a global BindableEvent that fires whenever a new actor is added to the game and its global state has been set up. This allows you to automatically run code on new actors as they're created.

[Event Arguments](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#event-arguments)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Argument | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `actor` | `Actor` | The actor instance that was added |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_added.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        print("New actor added:", actor:GetFullName())
    end)

[Auto-Setup Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#auto-setup-actors)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Automatically run setup code on all new actors
    on_actor_added.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        run_on_actor(actor, [[\
            -- Setup code for each actor\
            print("Actor initialized!")\
        ]])
    end)

[With Communication Channel](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#with-communication-channel)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    channel.Event:Connect(function(actorName)
        print("Actor ready:", actorName)
    end)
    
    on_actor_added.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        run_on_actor(actor, [[\
            local channelId = ...\
            local channel = get_comm_channel(channelId)\
            channel:Fire(script:GetFullName())\
        ]], id)
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fires only after the actor's global state is fully initialized
*   Useful for setting up hooks or injecting code into new actors

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors)
     - Get all existing actors
*   [`run_on_actor`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor)
     - Run code on an actor

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/isparallel)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created)

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added#syntax)

# Volt Documentation

[Crypt](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt)

crypt.random
============

Generates cryptographically secure random bytes.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------

    crypt.random(length: number) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `length` | `number` | Number of random bytes to generate |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | Random byte string |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------

`crypt.random` generates cryptographically secure random bytes, suitable for security-sensitive operations.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#example)

----------------------------------------------------------

    -- Generate 16 random bytes
    local randomBytes = crypt.random(16)
    print("Random bytes length:", #randomBytes)
    
    -- Convert to hex for display
    local hex = ""
    for i = 1, #randomBytes do
        hex = hex .. string.format("%02x", string.byte(randomBytes, i))
    end
    print("Hex:", hex)

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#use-cases)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   Generating session tokens
*   Creating random IVs for encryption
*   Generating salts for password hashing

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/random#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`crypt.generatebytes`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatebytes)
     - Alias for random bytes
*   [`crypt.generatekey`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/generatekey)
     - Generate encryption key

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/crypt/hmac)

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

rconsolehide
============

Hides and destroys the console window.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsolehide() -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `rconsoledestroy`
*   `consoledestroy`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsolehide` hides the console window and destroys it. All console output is cleared.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Show console and print something
    rconsoleshow()
    rconsoleprint("This console will close in 5 seconds...\n")
    
    -- Wait and then hide
    task.wait(5)
    rconsolehide()

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   All console content is lost when hidden
*   A new console can be created after hiding

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

hookmetamethod
==============

Hooks a metamethod on an object's metatable.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    hookmetamethod(object: any, metamethod: string, hook: function) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `object` | `any` | An object with the target metatable |
| `metamethod` | `string` | The metamethod name (e.g., "\*\*index", "\*\*namecall") |
| `hook` | `function` | The replacement function |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A reference to the original metamethod |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`hookmetamethod` replaces a metamethod in an object's metatable with your custom function. This is commonly used to intercept method calls, property accesses, and other metamethod operations on Roblox instances.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook __namecall to intercept method calls
    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
    
        if method == "GetService" then
            print("GetService called with:", ...)
        end
    
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))
    
    -- This triggers the hook
    local players = game:GetService("Players")

[Common Metamethods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#common-metamethods)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metamethod | Triggered By |
| --- | --- |
| `__index` | Property reads (`obj.Property`) |
| `__newindex` | Property writes (`obj.Property = value`) |
| `__namecall` | Method calls (`obj:Method()`) |
| `__tostring` | `tostring(obj)` |
| `__eq` | Equality comparison (`obj1 == obj2`) |

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Automatically uses `newcclosure` when hooking metamethods on Roblox objects
*   Use `getnamecallmethod` inside `__namecall` hooks to get the method name
*   Multiple objects may share the same metatable
*   Use `checkcaller` to filter volt vs game calls

[hookfunction\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction)
[iscclosure\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#example)
[Common Metamethods](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod#common-metamethods)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

run\_on\_actor
==============

Runs a script on an actor's state.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    run_on_actor(actor: Actor, script: string, ...: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `actor` | `Actor` | The actor to run the script on |
| `script` | `string` | The Lua code to execute |
| `...` | `any` | Arguments passed to the script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`run_on_actor` executes the provided script string on the specified actor's Luau state. This allows you to run code in parallel on different threads.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    local actor = Instance.new("Actor")
    actor.Parent = workspace
    
    run_on_actor(actor, [[\
        print("Hello from actor!")\
        print("Arguments:", ...)\
    ]], "arg1", "arg2")

[With Communication Channel](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#with-communication-channel)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    channel.Event:Connect(function(message)
        print("Received:", message)
    end)
    
    run_on_actor(Instance.new("Actor"), [[\
        local channelId = ...\
        local channel = get_comm_channel(channelId)\
        channel:Fire("Hello from actor!")\
    ]], id)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#notes)

-------------------------------------------------------------

*   The script runs in the actor's isolated environment
*   Use communication channels to send data back
*   Arguments are passed via varargs (`...`)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getactors`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactors)
     - Get all actors
*   [`create_comm_channel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/create_comm_channel)
     - Create communication channel

[on\_actor\_state\_created\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/cache)

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

getproperties
=============

Gets all properties of an instance.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    getproperties(instance: Instance) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Dictionary of all property values |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getproperties` returns a table containing all properties (both visible and hidden) and their current values for an instance.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = Instance.new("Part")
    local properties = getproperties(part)
    
    for property, value in pairs(properties) do
        print(property, "=", tostring(value))
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/getproperties#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`gethiddenproperties`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperties)
     - Get hidden only
*   [`gethiddenproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty)
     - Get single hidden property

# Volt Documentation

[Signals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

getsignalargumentsinfo
======================

Gets detailed information about a signal's expected arguments.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    getsignalargumentsinfo(signal: RBXScriptSignal) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `signal` | `RBXScriptSignal` | The signal to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of argument information entries |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getsignalargumentsinfo` returns detailed information about each argument a signal expects, including argument names and types.

[Return Structure](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#return-structure)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each entry in the returned array contains:

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Type` | `string` | The type name of the argument |
| `Name` | `string` | The parameter name |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local Players = game:GetService("Players")
    local argsInfo = getsignalargumentsinfo(Players.PlayerAdded)
    
    print("PlayerAdded arguments:")
    for i, arg in ipairs(argsInfo) do
        print(string.format("  %d. %s: %s", i, arg.Name, arg.Type))
    end

[Output Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#output-example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    PlayerAdded arguments:
      1. player: Player

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#use-cases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Understanding signal argument structure
*   Building dynamic signal handlers
*   Debugging signal connections

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getsignalarguments`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalarguments)
     - Get argument type names only
*   [`firesignal`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/firesignal)
     - Fire a signal

\

# Volt Documentation

[Input](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input)

keypress
========

Simulates pressing a keyboard key.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    keypress(keycode: number) -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   `keytap`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `keycode` | `number` | Virtual key code to press |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`keypress` simulates pressing a keyboard key down. The key stays pressed until `keyrelease` is called.

[Common Key Codes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#common-key-codes)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Key | Code |
| --- | --- |
| Space | `0x20` |
| Enter | `0x0D` |
| Escape | `0x1B` |
| Shift | `0x10` |
| Control | `0x11` |
| A-Z | `0x41-0x5A` |
| 0-9 | `0x30-0x39` |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Press and release the W key
    keypress(0x57)
    task.wait(0.5)
    keyrelease(0x57)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------

*   Use Windows virtual key codes
*   Always release keys that you press
*   Check `iswindowactive()` before simulating input

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keypress#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`keyrelease`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keyrelease)
     - Release a key
*   [`keyclick`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keyclick)
     - Press and release

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keyclick)
[keyrelease\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/keyrelease)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

fireproximityprompt
===================

Triggers a ProximityPrompt as if it was activated.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    fireproximityprompt(prompt: ProximityPrompt, amount?: number, skip?: boolean) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `prompt` | `ProximityPrompt` | The ProximityPrompt to fire |
| `amount` | `number?` | Number of times to trigger (default: 1) |
| `skip` | `boolean?` | Skip the hold duration (default: true) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`fireproximityprompt` simulates activation of a ProximityPrompt, bypassing distance and hold time requirements.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find a ProximityPrompt
    local prompt = workspace.Door.ProximityPrompt
    
    -- Fire it once
    fireproximityprompt(prompt)
    
    -- Fire it 5 times
    fireproximityprompt(prompt, 5)
    
    -- Fire without skipping hold duration
    fireproximityprompt(prompt, 1, false)

[Auto-Activate All Prompts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#auto-activate-all-prompts)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function fireAllPrompts(parent)
        for _, desc in ipairs(parent:GetDescendants()) do
            if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                fireproximityprompt(desc)
            end
        end
    end
    
    fireAllPrompts(workspace)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   By default, the hold duration is skipped
*   The `amount` parameter is useful for prompts that need multiple activations

[fireclickdetector\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireclickdetector)
[firetouchinterest\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest)

### On this page

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getloadedmodules
================

Returns all currently loaded ModuleScripts.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    getloadedmodules() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of loaded ModuleScripts |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getloadedmodules` returns a table of all ModuleScripts that have been required and loaded into memory.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local modules = getloadedmodules()
    print("Loaded modules:", #modules)
    
    for _, module in ipairs(modules) do
        print("-", module:GetFullName())
    end

[Finding Specific Modules](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#finding-specific-modules)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function findModule(name)
        for _, module in ipairs(getloadedmodules()) do
            if module.Name == name then
                return module
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    
    local playerModule = findModule("PlayerModule")
    if playerModule then
        print("Found PlayerModule:", playerModule:GetFullName())
    end

[Accessing Module Environments](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#accessing-module-environments)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    for _, module in ipairs(getloadedmodules()) do
        local env = getsenv(module)
        if env then
            print("Module:", module.Name)
            for key, value in pairs(env) do
                print("  ", key, type(value))
            end
        end
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getrunningscripts`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getrunningscripts)
     - Get running scripts
*   [`getsenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)
     - Get a script's environment

[getcallingscript\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript)
[getmodules\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules#returns)

# Volt Documentation

[Actors](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors)

on\_actor\_state\_created
=========================

Event fired when an Actor Lua state is created, before any scripts are executed.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_state_created: BindableEvent

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`on_actor_state_created` is a global BindableEvent that fires when a new Actor Lua state is created, before any scripts are executed on that state. This allows you to set up hooks or inject code into new actor states as they're created.

[Event Arguments](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#event-arguments)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Argument | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `actor` | `Actor` | The Actor instance whose state was created |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_state_created.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        print("New actor state created:", actor:GetFullName())
        
        -- Get the state for this actor
        local state = getluastate(actor)
        print("State ID:", state.Id)
    end)

[Setup Hooks on New States](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#setup-hooks-on-new-states)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    on_actor_state_created.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        local state = getluastate(actor)
        
        -- Execute setup code on the new state
        state:Execute([[\
            -- This runs before any scripts execute on the actor\
            print("Actor state initialized!")\
        ]])
    end)

[With Communication Channel](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#with-communication-channel)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local id, channel = create_comm_channel()
    channel.Event:Connect(function(actorName)
        print("Actor state ready:", actorName)
    end)
    
    on_actor_state_created.Event:Connect(function(actor)
        local state = getluastate(actor)
        state:Execute([[\
            local channelId = ...\
            local channel = get_comm_channel(channelId)\
            channel:Fire(script:GetFullName())\
        ]], id)
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fires before any scripts execute on the actor state
*   Useful for setting up hooks or injecting code early
*   The state is fully initialized but empty when this fires

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_state_created#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate)
     - Get LuaStateProxy for an actor
*   [`on_actor_added`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added)
     - Event fired when actor is ready (after scripts load)
*   [`getactorstates`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getactorstates)
     - Get all active LuaStateProxy objects

[on\_actor\_added\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/on_actor_added)
[run\_on\_actor\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/run_on_actor)

# Volt Documentation

[LuaStateProxy](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy)

LuaStateProxy.new
=================

Constructs a new LuaStateProxy based on the current Lua state.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    LuaStateProxy.new() -> LuaStateProxy

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

This function takes no parameters.

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `LuaStateProxy` | A new LuaStateProxy for the current state |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`LuaStateProxy.new` creates a new `LuaStateProxy` instance representing the current Lua execution state. This allows you to access state properties and execute code on the current state.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a proxy for the current state
    local state = LuaStateProxy.new()
    print("State ID:", state.Id)
    print("Is Actor State:", state.IsActorState)

[Get Current State](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#get-current-state)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local state = LuaStateProxy.new()
    
    -- Access state properties
    print("State ID:", state.Id)
    
    -- Execute code on this state
    state:Execute([[\
        print("Executed on current state!")\
    ]])

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/new#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getluastate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getluastate)
     - Get LuaStateProxy for an actor or script
*   [`getgamestate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/actors/getgamestate)
     - Get the default game Lua state
*   [`LuaStateProxy:Execute`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/luastateproxy/execute)
     - Execute code on the state

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

dofile
======

Loads and executes a Lua file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    dofile(path: string) -> any...

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#aliases)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   `runfile`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | Path to the Lua file |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any...` | Values returned by the executed file |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`dofile` reads a Lua file from the workspace folder, compiles it, and executes it. Any values returned by the file are returned by `dofile`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a script file
    writefile("mymodule.lua", [[\
        local module = {}\
        module.greeting = "Hello!"\
        return module\
    ]])
    
    -- Execute and get the return value
    local myModule = dofile("mymodule.lua")
    print(myModule.greeting) -- "Hello!"

[Execute Script](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#execute-script)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create and run a script
    writefile("script.lua", [[\
        print("Script executed!")\
        for i = 1, 5 do\
            print("Count:", i)\
        end\
    ]])
    
    dofile("script.lua")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------

*   This is a yielding function
*   File must be valid Lua/Luau code
*   Errors in the file will propagate

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`loadfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile)
     - Load without executing
*   [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
     - Read file as string

[delfolder\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder)
[getcustomasset\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile#returns)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getinfo
=============

Gets information about a function or stack level.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getinfo(func_or_level: function | number, what: string?) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func_or_level` | `function/number` | Function or stack level |
| `what` | `string` | (Optional) What info to return |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Information about target |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getinfo` returns a table with information about a function or the function at a given stack level.

[Info Fields](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#info-fields)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | What | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `name` | `n` | Function name |
| `source` | `S` | Source identifier |
| `short_src` | `S` | Short source name |
| `what` | `S` | "Lua", "C", or "main" |
| `currentline` | `l` | Current line |
| `linedefined` | `S` | Line where definition starts |
| `lastlinedefined` | `S` | Line where definition ends |
| `nups` | `u` | Number of upvalues |
| `nparams` | `u` | Number of parameters |
| `func` | `f` | The function itself |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    local function myFunc()
        return "hello"
    end
    
    local info = debug.getinfo(myFunc)
    print("Name:", info.name)
    print("Source:", info.short_src)
    print("Line defined:", info.linedefined)
    
    -- Get info for current function
    local currentInfo = debug.getinfo(1)
    print("Current function:", currentInfo.name)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getcallstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getcallstack)
     - Get full call stack
*   [`debug.validlevel`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel)
     - Check if level is valid

[debug.getconstants\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants)
[debug.getproto\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto)

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

iscclosure
==========

Checks if a function is a C closure.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    iscclosure(func: function) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the function is a C closure, `false` otherwise |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`iscclosure` returns whether the given function is implemented in C/C++ rather than Luau. C closures include built-in Lua functions, Roblox API methods, and functions wrapped with `newcclosure`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Built-in functions are C closures
    print(iscclosure(print)) -- true
    print(iscclosure(type)) -- true
    print(iscclosure(game.GetService)) -- true
    
    -- User-defined functions are Luau closures
    local function myFunc()
        return "hello"
    end
    print(iscclosure(myFunc)) -- false
    
    -- Wrapped functions become C closures
    local wrapped = newcclosure(myFunc)
    print(iscclosure(wrapped)) -- true

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`islclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure)
     - Check if a function is a Luau closure
*   [`newcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure)
     - Wrap a Luau function as a C closure

[hookmetamethod\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod)
[isexecutorclosure\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#example)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

makereadonly
============

Makes a table read-only.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    makereadonly(table: table) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `table` | `table` | The table to make read-only |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`makereadonly` sets a table's read-only flag to true, preventing modifications.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local myTable = {value = 123}
    
    makereadonly(myTable)
    
    -- This will error
    myTable.value = 456 -- Cannot modify read-only table

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Equivalent to `setreadonly(table, true)`
*   Use `makewritable` to reverse

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`makewritable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable)
     - Make table writable
*   [`setreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly)
     - Set read-only status
*   [`isreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)
     - Check read-only status

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/iswritable)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable)

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

makewritable
============

Makes a table writable.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    makewritable(table: table) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `table` | `table` | The table to make writable |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`makewritable` removes the read-only flag from a table, allowing modifications.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    -- Make writable for modifications
    makewritable(mt)
    
    -- Now we can modify it
    local oldIndex = mt.__index
    mt.__index = newcclosure(function(self, key)
        return oldIndex(self, key)
    end)
    
    -- Lock it again
    makereadonly(mt)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Equivalent to `setreadonly(table, false)`
*   Always re-lock metatables after modification

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makewritable#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`makereadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly)
     - Make table read-only
*   [`setreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly)
     - Set read-only status
*   [`isreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)
     - Check read-only status

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/makereadonly)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod)

# Volt Documentation

[Signals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

getsignalwhitelist
==================

Gets the list of signals in the network whitelist filter.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    getsignalwhitelist() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of whitelisted signal information |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getsignalwhitelist` returns information about signals that are in Roblox's strict network filter whitelist. These are signals that are allowed to replicate to the server.

[Return Structure](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#return-structure)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each entry in the returned array contains:

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Event` | `string` | The name of the event/signal |
| `Parent` | `string` | The class that owns the signal |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local whitelist = getsignalwhitelist()
    
    for i, entry in ipairs(whitelist) do
        print(string.format("%s.%s", entry.Parent, entry.Event))
    end

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#use-cases)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Determining which signals can be replicated
*   Understanding network security boundaries
*   Debugging replication issues

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalwhitelist#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`replicatesignal`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal)
     - Fire with replication
*   [`cansignalreplicate`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/cansignalreplicate)
     - Check if signal can replicate

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/getsignalargumentsinfo)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal)

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

getcustomasset
==============

Returns a content URL for a local file that can be used in Roblox.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    getcustomasset(path: string) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | A content URL usable in Roblox |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getcustomasset` converts a local file into a content URL that Roblox can use for images, sounds, and other assets.

[Example: Custom Image](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#example-custom-image)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Save an image to the workspace
    -- (assume image data is obtained somehow)
    writefile("myimage.png", imageData)
    
    -- Get a usable URL
    local imageUrl = getcustomasset("myimage.png")
    
    -- Use it in a GUI
    local imageLabel = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
    imageLabel.Image = imageUrl
    imageLabel.Parent = someGui

[Example: Custom Sound](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#example-custom-sound)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Get URL for a local sound file
    local soundUrl = getcustomasset("mysound.mp3")
    
    -- Create and play the sound
    local sound = Instance.new("Sound")
    sound.SoundId = soundUrl
    sound.Parent = workspace
    sound:Play()

[Supported Formats](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#supported-formats)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Formats |
| --- | --- |
| Images | PNG, JPG, JPEG |
| Audio | MP3, OGG, WAV |

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#notes)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The file must exist in the workspace folder
*   The returned URL is only valid for the current session
*   Large files may take time to load

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/getcustomasset#aliases)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `getsynasset`

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/dofile)

# Volt Documentation

[Console](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console)

rconsoleinput
=============

Gets input from the user via the console.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleinput() -> string

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#aliases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `consoleinput`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The user's input |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsoleinput` waits for the user to type something in the console and press Enter, then returns the input as a string. This is a yielding function.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleshow()
    
    rconsoleprint("What is your name? ")
    local name = rconsoleinput()
    
    rconsoleprint("Hello, " .. name .. "!\n")

[Interactive Menu Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#interactive-menu-example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleshow()
    rconsolename("Script Menu")
    
    rconsoleprint("Select an option:\n")
    rconsoleprint("1. Option A\n")
    rconsoleprint("2. Option B\n")
    rconsoleprint("3. Exit\n\n")
    rconsoleprint("Enter choice: ")
    
    local choice = rconsoleinput()
    
    if choice == "1" then
        rconsoleprint("You selected Option A\n")
    elseif choice == "2" then
        rconsoleprint("You selected Option B\n")
    else
        rconsoleprint("Goodbye!\n")
        task.wait(1)
        rconsolehide()
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   This function yields until the user presses Enter
*   Returns an empty string if the console is closed

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinput#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`rconsoleprint`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint)
     - Print to console

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleinfo)
