# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

isnetworkowner
==============

Checks if the local player owns a part's physics simulation.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    isnetworkowner(part: BasePart) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `part` | `BasePart` | The part to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if local player is network owner |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isnetworkowner` checks whether the local client has network ownership of a part, meaning they control its physics simulation.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = workspace.Part
    
    if isnetworkowner(part) then
        print("You own this part's physics")
        -- Can manipulate physics reliably
        part.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 50, 0)
    else
        print("Server or another player owns this part")
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#notes)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Network ownership affects physics simulation authority
*   Use `setsimulationradius` to expand ownership range

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isnetworkowner#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`setsimulationradius`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius)
     - Set simulation radius

# Volt Documentation

[Signals](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

replicatesignal
===============

Fires a signal with server replication.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    replicatesignal(signal: RBXScriptSignal, ...: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `signal` | `RBXScriptSignal` | The signal to fire |
| `...` | `any` | Arguments to pass |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`replicatesignal` fires a signal in a way that replicates to the server, unlike `firesignal` which only fires locally.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Fire a ProximityPrompt's Triggered signal with replication
    local prompt = workspace.Door.ProximityPrompt
    replicatesignal(prompt.Triggered, game.Players.LocalPlayer)

[Difference from firesignal](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#difference-from-firesignal)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Function | Local | Replicates |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `firesignal` | ✅   | ❌   |
| `replicatesignal` | ✅   | ✅   |

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#use-cases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Input simulation**: Simulate user input that needs server acknowledgment
*   **Interaction triggers**: Fire interaction events that should replicate
*   **Testing**: Test server-replicated behavior

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Not all signals can be replicated
*   Server validation may still reject the action

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals/replicatesignal#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

getfpscap
=========

Gets the current FPS cap.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/getfpscap#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    getfpscap() -> number

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/getfpscap#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `number` | Current FPS cap |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/getfpscap#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getfpscap` returns the current maximum FPS setting.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/getfpscap#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    local currentCap = getfpscap()
    print("Current FPS cap:", currentCap)
    
    -- Toggle between capped and uncapped
    if currentCap == 0 then
        setfpscap(60)
    else
        setfpscap(0)
    end

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getproto
==============

Gets a proto (nested function) from a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getproto(func: function | number, index: number, activated?: boolean) -> function | table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |
| `index` | `number` | The proto index (1-based) |
| `activated` | `boolean?` | If true, returns all activated instances |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | The proto at the specified index (if `activated` is false/nil) |
| `table` | Array of activated instances (if `activated` is true) |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getproto` retrieves a nested function definition (proto) from within a function. Protos are functions defined inside other functions.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    local function outer()
        local function inner1()
            print("inner1")
        end
        
        local function inner2()
            print("inner2")
        end
        
        inner1()
        inner2()
    end
    
    -- Get the first nested function
    local proto1 = debug.getproto(outer, 1)
    proto1() -- Output: inner1
    
    -- Get the second nested function
    local proto2 = debug.getproto(outer, 2)
    proto2() -- Output: inner2

[Activated Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#activated-instances)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When `activated` is true, returns all instances of the proto that have been created:

    local instances = {}
    
    local function factory()
        local function create()
            return {}
        end
        table.insert(instances, create())
        table.insert(instances, create())
    end
    
    factory()
    
    -- Get all activated instances of the inner function
    local activated = debug.getproto(factory, 1, true)
    print(#activated) -- Number of times the inner function was instantiated

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getprotos`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos)
     - Get all protos from a function

[debug.getinfo\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getinfo)
[debug.getprotos\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#example)
[Activated Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#activated-instances)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto#related-functions)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

firetouchinterest
=================

Triggers a Touched or TouchEnded event between two parts.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    firetouchinterest(part: BasePart, target: BasePart, toggle: number) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `part` | `BasePart` | The touching part |
| `target` | `BasePart` | The part to touch |
| `toggle` | `number` | 0 = TouchEnded, 1 = Touched |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`firetouchinterest` simulates a touch between two parts, firing the Touched or TouchEnded events without physical contact.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    local hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
    local targetPart = workspace.TouchPart
    
    -- Simulate touch start
    firetouchinterest(hrp, targetPart, 1)
    
    -- Simulate touch end
    firetouchinterest(hrp, targetPart, 0)

[Touch and Release](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#touch-and-release)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function touch(part, target)
        firetouchinterest(part, target, 1) -- Touch
        task.wait()
        firetouchinterest(part, target, 0) -- Release
    end
    
    touch(hrp, workspace.Coin)

[Collecting Items](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#collecting-items)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function collectTouchParts(parent)
        local hrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
        
        for _, part in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                firetouchinterest(hrp, part, 1)
                task.wait()
                firetouchinterest(hrp, part, 0)
            end
        end
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Toggle: 1 = Touched (start), 0 = TouchEnded (end)
*   Both events should be fired for proper simulation

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/fireproximityprompt)
[getcallbackvalue\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/firetouchinterest#description)

getmodules
==========

Gets all ModuleScripts in the game.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    getmodules() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of all ModuleScripts |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getmodules` returns an array of all ModuleScripts in the game, including those that haven't been required yet.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local modules = getmodules()
    print("Total modules:", #modules)
    
    -- Find a specific module
    for _, module in ipairs(modules) do
        if module.Name == "Settings" then
            print("Found Settings module at:", module:GetFullName())
        end
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns all ModuleScripts, not just loaded ones
*   Use `getloadedmodules` for only required modules

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getmodules#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getloadedmodules`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getloadedmodules)
     - Get loaded modules only
*   [`getscripts`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts)
     - Get all scripts

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

isexecutorclosure
=================

Checks if a function originates from volt.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    isexecutorclosure(func: function) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the function is from volt, `false` otherwise |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isexecutorclosure` determines whether a function was created by or is part of volt's environment. This includes both volt-provided functions (like `loadstring`, `hookfunction`) and functions defined in your scripts.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Volt functions return true
    print(isexecutorclosure(loadstring)) -- true
    print(isexecutorclosure(hookfunction)) -- true
    
    -- Your script functions return true
    local function myFunc()
        return "hello"
    end
    print(isexecutorclosure(myFunc)) -- true
    
    -- Game functions return false
    print(isexecutorclosure(print)) -- false
    print(isexecutorclosure(game.GetService)) -- false

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`checkcaller`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/checkcaller)
     - Check if the current call is from volt's thread
*   [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
     - Check if a function is a C closure
*   [`islclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure)
     - Check if a function is a Luau closure

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isexecutorclosure#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `checkclosure`
*   `isourclosure`

[iscclosure\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
[isfunctionhooked\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked)

getrunningscripts

    local function listRunningScripts()
        local scripts = getrunningscripts()
        
        print("=== Running Scripts ===")
        for i, script in ipairs(scripts) do
            print(i, script.Name, script:GetFullName())
        end
        print("Total:", #scripts)
    end
    
    listRunningScripts()

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

getcallbackvalue
================

Gets the function assigned to a callback property.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    getcallbackvalue(instance: Instance, property: string) -> function?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance |
| `property` | `string` | The callback property name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function?` | The callback function, or nil if not set |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getcallbackvalue` retrieves the function assigned to a callback property like `OnInvoke` or `OnClientEvent`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a BindableFunction
    local bindable = Instance.new("BindableFunction")
    bindable.OnInvoke = function(arg)
        return arg * 2
    end
    
    -- Get the callback
    local callback = getcallbackvalue(bindable, "OnInvoke")
    print(callback(5)) -- 10

[Inspecting Remote Callbacks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#inspecting-remote-callbacks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find RemoteFunction callbacks
    for _, obj in ipairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
            local callback = getcallbackvalue(obj, "OnClientInvoke")
            if callback then
                print("Found callback on:", obj:GetFullName())
            end
        end
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Common callback properties: `OnInvoke`, `OnClientInvoke`, `OnServerInvoke`
*   Returns nil if no callback is set

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getcallbackvalue#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

gethui
======

Returns the hidden UI container.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/gethui#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    gethui() -> Instance

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/gethui#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Instance` | The hidden UI container |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/gethui#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`gethui` returns a special container for UI that is hidden from game scripts.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/gethui#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    gui.Name = "MyHiddenGui"
    gui.Parent = gethui()
    
    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 100)
    frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -100, 0.5, -50)
    frame.Parent = gui

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/gethui#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------

*   Use for UIs you want to hide from being accessed by a game script
*   The container behaves like a normal GUI container

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getscriptbytecode
=================

Gets the compiled bytecode of a script.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    getscriptbytecode(script: LocalScript | ModuleScript) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `script` | `LocalScript` or `ModuleScript` | The script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | The compiled Luau bytecode |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getscriptbytecode` extracts the compiled bytecode from a script. This can be used for analysis or decompilation.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local scripts = getrunningscripts()
    if #scripts > 0 then
        local bytecode = getscriptbytecode(scripts[1])
        print("Bytecode length:", #bytecode)
        
        -- Save to file for analysis
        writefile("script_bytecode.bin", bytecode)
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#notes)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Bytecode is in compiled Luau format
*   Can be decompiled with appropriate tools
*   Useful for script analysis and research

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getscripthash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash)
     - Get a hash of the bytecode
*   [`getscriptclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure)
     - Get the script's function

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode#aliases)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `dumpstring`

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

isscriptable
============

Checks if a property is scriptable.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    isscriptable(instance: Instance, property: string) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance |
| `property` | `string` | The property name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the property is scriptable |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isscriptable` checks whether a property can be accessed through scripts. Non-scriptable properties are hidden from the scripting API.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = Instance.new("Part")
    
    -- Check common properties
    print(isscriptable(part, "Name"))     -- true (visible)
    print(isscriptable(part, "Position")) -- true (visible)
    print(isscriptable(part, "size_xml")) -- false (hidden)

[Use Case](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#use-case)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function getAllProperties(instance)
        local properties = {}
        
        -- Check a list of known property names
        local propertyNames = {"Name", "Position", "Size", "Color", "size_xml"}
        
        for _, propName in ipairs(propertyNames) do
            local scriptable = isscriptable(instance, propName)
            properties[propName] = {
                scriptable = scriptable,
                value = scriptable and instance[propName] or gethiddenproperty(instance, propName)
            }
        end
        
        return properties
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`setscriptable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable)
     - Change scriptability
*   [`gethiddenproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty)
     - Get hidden property values

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

setrawmetatable
===============

Sets the raw metatable of an object.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    setrawmetatable(object: any, metatable: table?) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `object` | `any` | The object to modify |
| `metatable` | `table?` | The new metatable, or nil to remove |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setrawmetatable` sets the metatable of an object directly, bypassing normal restrictions.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local myTable = {}
    
    -- Create a custom metatable
    local mt = {
        __index = function(self, key)
            return "Key not found: " .. key
        end
    }
    
    setrawmetatable(myTable, mt)
    
    print(myTable.anything) -- "Key not found: anything"

[Replacing Metatables](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#replacing-metatables)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local object = {}
    local originalMt = getrawmetatable(object)
    
    -- Set a new metatable
    setrawmetatable(object, {
        __tostring = function()
            return "Custom string!"
        end
    })
    
    print(tostring(object)) -- "Custom string!"
    
    -- Restore original
    setrawmetatable(object, originalMt)

[Caution](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#caution)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Modifying metatables of Roblox objects can cause unexpected behavior or crashes. Always keep a reference to the original.

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable)
     - Get a raw metatable

Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly)

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

setnamecallmethod
=================

Sets the method name for the current `__namecall` invocation.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    setnamecallmethod(method: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `method` | `string` | The new method name |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setnamecallmethod` changes the method name that will be used for the current `__namecall` invocation. This allows you to redirect method calls to different methods.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
        
        -- Redirect Kick to a harmless method
        if method == "Kick" then
            setnamecallmethod("GetFullName")
            return oldNamecall(self, ...)
        end
        
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))

[Spoofing Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#spoofing-example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local oldNamecall
    oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
        local method = getnamecallmethod()
        
        -- Change FireServer to something else for debugging
        if method == "FireServer" then
            print("FireServer intercepted, redirecting...")
            setnamecallmethod("Fire")
        end
        
        return oldNamecall(self, ...)
    end))

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only works inside `__namecall` hooks
*   The change only affects the current call

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setnamecallmethod#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getnamecallmethod`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getnamecallmethod)
     - Get current method
*   [`hookmetamethod`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookmetamethod)
     - Hook metamethods

# Volt Documentation

[Metatable](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable)

setreadonly
===========

Sets a table's read-only status.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    setreadonly(table: table, readonly: boolean) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `table` | `table` | The table to modify |
| `readonly` | `boolean` | The new read-only status |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setreadonly` controls whether a table can be modified. This is essential for modifying Roblox metatables which are locked by default.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
    
    -- Unlock the metatable
    setreadonly(mt, false)
    
    -- Now we can modify it
    local oldIndex = mt.__index
    mt.__index = newcclosure(function(self, key)
        print("Accessing:", key)
        return oldIndex(self, key)
    end)
    
    -- Re-lock for safety
    setreadonly(mt, true)

[Pattern for Safe Modification](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#pattern-for-safe-modification)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeModifyMetatable(object, modifier)
        local mt = getrawmetatable(object)
        local wasReadonly = isreadonly(mt)
        
        if wasReadonly then
            setreadonly(mt, false)
        end
        
        modifier(mt)
        
        if wasReadonly then
            setreadonly(mt, true)
        end
    end
    
    safeModifyMetatable(game, function(mt)
        -- Your modifications here
    end)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Always re-lock metatables after modification
*   Some anti-cheats check for unlocked metatables
*   Works on any Lua table, not just metatables

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isreadonly`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/isreadonly)
     - Check read-only status
*   [`getrawmetatable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/getrawmetatable)
     - Get the metatable

[setrawmetatable\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setrawmetatable)
[Miscellaneous\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/metatable/setreadonly#example)

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

isfunctionhooked
================

Checks if a function has been hooked.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    isfunctionhooked(func: function) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the function is hooked |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isfunctionhooked` checks whether a function has been replaced using `hookfunction` or similar hooking methods.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function myFunc()
        return "original"
    end
    
    print(isfunctionhooked(myFunc)) -- false
    
    hookfunction(myFunc, function()
        return "hooked"
    end)
    
    print(isfunctionhooked(myFunc)) -- true

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#use-cases)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Checking if a function has already been hooked
*   Avoiding double-hooking
*   Debugging hook states

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`hookfunction`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/hookfunction)
     - Hook a function
*   [`restorefunction`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction)
     - Restore original

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

isfile
======

Checks if a path points to a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    isfile(path: string) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The path to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the path is a file |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`isfile` returns whether the specified path exists and is a file (not a folder).

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    writefile("test.txt", "Hello")
    makefolder("testfolder")
    
    print(isfile("test.txt"))     -- true
    print(isfile("testfolder"))   -- false (it's a folder)
    print(isfile("nonexistent"))  -- false (doesn't exist)

[Safe File Reading](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#safe-file-reading)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeRead(path)
        if isfile(path) then
            return readfile(path)
        end
        return nil
    end
    
    local content = safeRead("config.json")
    if content then
        print("Config loaded")
    else
        print("Config not found")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder)
     - Check if path is a folder
*   [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
     - Read file contents

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

isfolder
========

Checks if a path points to a folder.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    isfolder(path: string) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The path to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the path is a folder |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isfolder` returns whether the specified path exists and is a folder (not a file).

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    makefolder("myfolder")
    writefile("myfile.txt", "Hello")
    
    print(isfolder("myfolder"))    -- true
    print(isfolder("myfile.txt"))  -- false (it's a file)
    print(isfolder("nonexistent")) -- false (doesn't exist)

[Ensuring Folder Exists](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#ensuring-folder-exists)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function ensureFolder(path)
        if not isfolder(path) then
            makefolder(path)
        end
    end
    
    ensureFolder("data")
    ensureFolder("data/saves")
    writefile("data/saves/save1.json", "{}")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile)
     - Check if path is a file
*   [`makefolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder)
     - Create a folder

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder#example)

# Volt Documentation

[Reflection](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection)

setscriptable
=============

Sets whether a property is scriptable.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    setscriptable(instance: Instance, property: string, scriptable: boolean) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `instance` | `Instance` | The instance |
| `property` | `string` | The property name |
| `scriptable` | `boolean` | The new scriptability |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | The previous scriptability |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setscriptable` changes whether a property is accessible through normal scripting. This can make hidden properties accessible via regular property access.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local part = Instance.new("Part")
    
    -- Make a hidden property scriptable
    local wasScriptable = setscriptable(part, "size_xml", true)
    
    -- Now we can access it normally
    print(part.size_xml)
    
    -- Restore original state
    setscriptable(part, "size_xml", wasScriptable)

[Making Hidden Properties Accessible](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#making-hidden-properties-accessible)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function exposeProperty(instance, propName)
        local wasScriptable = setscriptable(instance, propName, true)
        return function()
            setscriptable(instance, propName, wasScriptable)
        end
    end
    
    -- Use
    local restore = exposeProperty(part, "size_xml")
    print(part.size_xml) -- Now accessible
    restore() -- Restore original state

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isscriptable`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/isscriptable)
     - Check scriptability
*   [`gethiddenproperty`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/gethiddenproperty)
     - Alternative for hidden properties

[sethiddenproperty\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/sethiddenproperty)
[setsimulationradius\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setsimulationradius)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#example)
[Making Hidden Properties Accessible](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/reflection/setscriptable#making-hidden-properties-accessible)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getprotos
===============

Gets all protos (nested functions) from a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getprotos(func: function | number) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | An array of all protos in the function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getprotos` returns a table containing all nested function definitions within a function.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    local function container()
        local function a() return 1 end
        local function b() return 2 end
        local function c() return 3 end
        return a() + b() + c()
    end
    
    local protos = debug.getprotos(container)
    print(#protos) -- 3
    
    for i, proto in ipairs(protos) do
        print(i, proto()) -- Calls each nested function
    end
    --[[\
    Output:\
    1  1\
    2  2\
    3  3\
    ]]

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#use-cases)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Script analysis**: Find all functions defined within a script
*   **Hooking**: Locate specific nested functions to hook
*   **Debugging**: Inspect the structure of complex functions

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getproto`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto)
     - Get a single proto by index

[debug.getproto\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getproto)
[debug.getstack\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#example)
[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos#use-cases)

rconsoleprint
=============

Prints text to the console window.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint#syntax)

| --- | --- | --- |

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsoleprint` outputs text to the console window. Unlike the other console print functions, this prints plain text without any formatting or prefix.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleshow()
    
    -- Print text with newlines
    rconsoleprint("Hello, World!\n")
    rconsoleprint("Line 2\n")
    
    -- Print without newline (continues on same line)
    rconsoleprint("Part 1... ")
    rconsoleprint("Part 2\n")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint#notes)

---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use `\n` for newlines
*   Does not automatically add newlines

     - Print error

setfpscap

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#syntax)

    setfpscap(fps: number) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#parameters)

| --- | --- | --- |
| `fps` | `number` | The FPS cap to set |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`setfpscap` sets the maximum frames per second the game will render at. Use 0 to uncap.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Cap at 60 FPS
    setfpscap(60)
    
    -- Uncap FPS
    setfpscap(0)
    
    -- Cap at 144 FPS
    setfpscap(144)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/setfpscap#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Set to 0 for unlimited FPS
*   Higher FPS may increase CPU/GPU usage
*   Default Roblox cap is 60 FPS

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getstack
==============

Gets a value from the stack at a specific level and index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getstack(level: number, index: number) -> any

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `level` | `number` | The stack level (1 = current function) |
| `index` | `number` | The stack slot index |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The value at the specified stack position |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getstack` retrieves a value from the call stack. This allows you to read local variables and temporary values from any level of the current call stack.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    local function level2()
        local secret = "hidden value"
        level1()
    end
    
    local function level1()
        -- Get the 'secret' variable from level2
        local value = debug.getstack(2, 1)
        print(value) -- "hidden value"
    end
    
    level2()

[Stack Levels](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#stack-levels)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Level | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 1   | Current function |
| 2   | Calling function |
| 3   | Caller of the caller |
| ... | And so on |

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------

*   Stack indices correspond to local variable slots
*   The exact index depends on the function's compiled bytecode
*   Values may include locals, parameters, and temporaries

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.setstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack)
     - Modify a stack value

[debug.getprotos\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getprotos)
[debug.getupvalue\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#example)
[Stack Levels](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#stack-levels)
[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#notes)
[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Simulate dragging
    mouse1press()
    for i = 1, 100 do
        mousemoverel(5, 0)
        task.wait(0.01)
    end
    mouse1release()

# Volt Documentation

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

messagebox
==========

Displays a message box dialog.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    messagebox(text: string, caption: string, flags: number) -> number

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `text` | `string` | The message text |
| `caption` | `string` | The window title |
| `flags` | `number` | Button and icon flags |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `number` | The button pressed by the user |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`messagebox` displays a Windows-style message box with customizable buttons and icons.

[Common Flags](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#common-flags)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Flag | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `0` | OK button |
| `1` | OK + Cancel |
| `4` | Yes + No |
| `16` | Error icon |
| `32` | Question icon |
| `48` | Warning icon |
| `64` | Info icon |

[Return Values](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#return-values)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Value | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `1` | OK  |
| `2` | Cancel |
| `6` | Yes |
| `7` | No  |

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Simple message
    messagebox("Hello!", "Greeting", 0)
    
    -- Confirmation dialog
    local result = messagebox("Are you sure?", "Confirm", 4 + 32)
    if result == 6 then
        print("User clicked Yes")
    else
        print("User clicked No")
    end
    
    -- Warning message
    messagebox("Something went wrong!", "Warning", 0 + 48)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/messagebox#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Flags can be combined with addition
*   This is a yielding function

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getscriptclosure
================

Gets the main function of a script.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    getscriptclosure(script: LocalScript | ModuleScript) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `script` | `LocalScript` or `ModuleScript` | The script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | The script's main function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getscriptclosure` returns the main function (closure) of a script. For ModuleScripts, this is the function that would be returned by `require()`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local scripts = getrunningscripts()
    if #scripts > 0 then
        local closure = getscriptclosure(scripts[1])
        print("Got closure:", closure)
        
        -- Inspect the function
        local constants = debug.getconstants(closure)
        print("Constants:", #constants)
    end

[Accessing Module Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#accessing-module-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local modules = getloadedmodules()
    for _, module in ipairs(modules) do
        local closure = getscriptclosure(module)
        
        -- Get module's protos (inner functions)
        local protos = debug.getprotos(closure)
        print(module.Name, "has", #protos, "inner functions")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#related-functions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getscriptbytecode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode)
     - Get bytecode
*   [`getsenv`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)
     - Get script environment

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure#aliases)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `getscriptfunction`

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.validlevel
================

Checks if a stack level is valid.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.validlevel(level: number) -> boolean

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#aliases)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   `debug.isvalidlevel`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `level` | `number` | The stack level |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if the stack level is valid |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.validlevel` checks whether a given stack level exists and is valid for debugging operations.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/validlevel#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Check stack levels
    for i = 0, 10 do
        if debug.validlevel(i) then
            print("Level " .. i .. " is valid")
        else
            print("Level " .. i .. " is invalid")
            break
        end
    end

# Volt Documentation

[Input](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input)

mouse1release
=============

Simulates releasing the left mouse button.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1release#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    mouse1release() -> void

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1release#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1release#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`mouse1release` simulates releasing the left mouse button that was pressed with `mouse1press`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1release#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    mouse1press()
    task.wait(0.5)
    mouse1release()

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1release#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`mouse1press`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1press)
     - Press left mouse
*   [`mouse1click`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/input/mouse1click)
     - Click left mouse

# Volt Documentation

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

identifyexecutor
================

Returns information about volt.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    identifyexecutor() -> string, string

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | Volt |
| `string` | Version |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`identifyexecutor` returns the name and version of volt.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local name, version = identifyexecutor()
    print("Name:", name)
    print("Version:", version)
    -- Example output:
    -- Name: Volt
    -- Version: 1.0.0.0

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/identifyexecutor#aliases)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `getexecutorname`

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getscriptfromthread
===================

Gets the script associated with a thread.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    getscriptfromthread(thread: thread) -> LuaSourceContainer?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `thread` | `thread` | The thread to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `LuaSourceContainer?` | The script, or nil if none associated |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getscriptfromthread` returns the script (LocalScript, ModuleScript, or Script) that is running in the specified thread.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local script = getscriptfromthread(coroutine.running())
    if script then
        print("Current script:", script:GetFullName())
    end
    
    -- Check what script a connection is from
    local connection
    connection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        local thread = coroutine.running()
        local scriptSource = getscriptfromthread(thread)
        if scriptSource then
            print("Heartbeat from:", scriptSource.Name)
        end
        connection:Disconnect()
    end)

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getcallingscript`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getcallingscript)
     - Get calling script
*   [`getrunningscripts`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getrunningscripts)
     - Get all running scripts

[getscriptclosure\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptclosure)
[getscripthash\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash)

### On this page

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

getinstances
============

Returns all instances in the game.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    getinstances() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of all instances |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getinstances` returns a table containing every instance currently in the game, including those not in the DataModel hierarchy.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local instances = getinstances()
    print("Total instances:", #instances)
    
    -- Count by class
    local counts = {}
    for _, inst in ipairs(instances) do
        local class = inst.ClassName
        counts[class] = (counts[class] or 0) + 1
    end
    
    for class, count in pairs(counts) do
        print(class, count)
    end

[Finding Specific Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#finding-specific-instances)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find all Scripts
    local scripts = {}
    for _, inst in ipairs(getinstances()) do
        if inst:IsA("Script") then
            table.insert(scripts, inst)
        end
    end

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Returns a very large table
*   Includes nil-parented instances
*   May impact performance if called frequently

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getnilinstances`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances)
     - Get only nil-parented instances

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstancecache)
[getnilinstances\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#syntax)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#example)
[Finding Specific Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances#finding-specific-instances)

# Volt Documentation

[Instances](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances)

getnilinstances
===============

Returns all instances with nil parent.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

    getnilinstances() -> table

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of nil-parented instances |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getnilinstances` returns all instances that have their Parent set to nil. These instances exist in memory but aren't part of the game hierarchy.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

    local nilInstances = getnilinstances()
    print("Nil instances:", #nilInstances)
    
    for _, inst in ipairs(nilInstances) do
        print(inst.ClassName, inst.Name)
    end

[Finding Hidden Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#finding-hidden-scripts)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Scripts are sometimes hidden by setting parent to nil
    local hiddenScripts = {}
    for _, inst in ipairs(getnilinstances()) do
        if inst:IsA("LocalScript") or inst:IsA("ModuleScript") then
            table.insert(hiddenScripts, inst)
        end
    end
    
    print("Found", #hiddenScripts, "hidden scripts")

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#use-cases)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Finding hidden instances**: Locate instances games try to hide
*   **Script discovery**: Find scripts that were parented to nil
*   **Memory inspection**: See what's being kept in memory

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getnilinstances#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getinstances`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstances)
     - Get all instances

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

islclosure
==========

Checks if a function is a Luau closure.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    islclosure(func: function) -> boolean

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | `true` if the function is a Luau closure, `false` otherwise |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`islclosure` returns whether the given function is written in Luau rather than C/C++. Luau closures include user-defined functions and script functions.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- User-defined functions are Luau closures
    local function myFunc()
        return "hello"
    end
    print(islclosure(myFunc)) -- true
    
    -- Built-in functions are NOT Luau closures
    print(islclosure(print)) -- false
    print(islclosure(type)) -- false
    
    -- Wrapped functions are NOT Luau closures
    local wrapped = newcclosure(myFunc)
    print(islclosure(wrapped)) -- false

[Relationship with iscclosure](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#relationship-with-iscclosure)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`islclosure` is the logical opposite of `iscclosure`:

    local function test() end
    
    print(islclosure(test)) -- true
    print(iscclosure(test)) -- false
    
    print(islclosure(test) == not iscclosure(test)) -- true

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
     - Check if a function is a C closure
*   [`newcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure)
     - Convert a Luau closure to a C closure

[isfunctionhooked\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isfunctionhooked)
[isnewcclosure\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#example)
[Relationship with iscclosure](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure#relationship-with-iscclosure)

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

isnewcclosure
=============

Checks if a function is a newcclosure wrapper.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    isnewcclosure(func: function) -> boolean

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#aliases)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `iscustomcclosure`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The function to check |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `boolean` | True if function was created by newcclosure |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`isnewcclosure` checks whether a function was wrapped using `newcclosure`.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function luaFunc()
        return "lua"
    end
    
    local wrapped = newcclosure(luaFunc)
    
    print(isnewcclosure(luaFunc)) -- false
    print(isnewcclosure(wrapped)) -- true
    print(isnewcclosure(print))   -- false (native C closure)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   Useful for distinguishing between native C closures and wrapped functions
*   Returns false for native C closures like `print`

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`newcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure)
     - Wrap as C closure
*   [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
     - Check if C closure
*   [`islclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure)
     - Check if Luau closure

\

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getupvalue
================

Gets an upvalue from a function by index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getupvalue(func: function | number, index: number) -> any

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#parameters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |
| `index` | `number` | The upvalue index (1-based) |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `any` | The upvalue at the specified index |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getupvalue` retrieves an upvalue (captured variable from an outer scope) from a function. Upvalues are variables that a closure "closes over" from its enclosing environment.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    local counter = 0
    local prefix = "Count: "
    
    local function increment()
        counter = counter + 1
        return prefix .. counter
    end
    
    -- Get the upvalues
    print(debug.getupvalue(increment, 1)) -- 0 (counter)
    print(debug.getupvalue(increment, 2)) -- "Count: " (prefix)
    
    -- After calling the function
    increment()
    print(debug.getupvalue(increment, 1)) -- 1 (counter was modified)

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#use-cases)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Inspect closures**: See what variables a function has captured
*   **Debugging**: Examine the state of captured variables
*   **Modification**: Read before modifying with `setupvalue`

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getupvalues`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues)
     - Get all upvalues
*   [`debug.setupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue)
     - Modify an upvalue

[debug.getstack\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack)
[debug.getupvalues\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue#example)
