[Console](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console)

rconsoleshow
============

Creates and shows the console window.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoleshow() -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#aliases)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `rconsolecreate`
*   `consolecreate`

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsoleshow` creates a new console window if one doesn't exist, and shows it. The console can be used to display output and receive user input.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create and show the console
    rconsoleshow()
    
    -- Print a welcome message
    rconsoleprint("Welcome to the console!\n")
    
    -- Set a custom title
    rconsolename("My Script Console")

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only one console window can exist at a time
*   The console persists until `rconsolehide` is called or the game closes
*   Use `\n` for newlines in console output

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`rconsolehide`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide)
     - Hide the console
*   [`rconsoleprint`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint)
     - Print to console
*   [`rconsolename`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolename)
     - Set console title

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleprint)

\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle)

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

listfiles
=========

Lists all files and folders in a directory.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    listfiles(path: string) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The folder path |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Array of file and folder paths |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`listfiles` returns a table containing the paths of all files and folders within the specified directory.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create some files and folders
    makefolder("mydata")
    writefile("mydata/file1.txt", "Hello")
    writefile("mydata/file2.txt", "World")
    makefolder("mydata/subfolder")
    
    -- List contents
    local files = listfiles("mydata")
    for _, path in ipairs(files) do
        print(path)
    end
    --[[\
    mydata/file1.txt\
    mydata/file2.txt\
    mydata/subfolder\
    ]]

[Filtering Files and Folders](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#filtering-files-and-folders)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function getFiles(path)
        local files = {}
        for _, item in ipairs(listfiles(path)) do
            if isfile(item) then
                table.insert(files, item)
            end
        end
        return files
    end
    
    local function getFolders(path)
        local folders = {}
        for _, item in ipairs(listfiles(path)) do
            if isfolder(item) then
                table.insert(folders, item)
            end
        end
        return folders
    end

[Recursive Listing](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#recursive-listing)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function listAllFiles(path, results)
        results = results or {}
        for _, item in ipairs(listfiles(path)) do
            if isfile(item) then
                table.insert(results, item)
            elseif isfolder(item) then
                listAllFiles(item, results)
            end
        end
        return results
    end
    
    local allFiles = listAllFiles("mydata")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfile)
     - Check if path is a file
*   [`isfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder)
     - Check if path is a folder

[isfolder\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder)
[loadfile\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#example)
[Filtering Files and Folders](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles#filtering-files-and-folders)

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

loadstring
==========

Compiles a string of Lua code and returns it as a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------

    loadstring(code: string, chunkname?: string) -> function?, string?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `code` | `string` | The Lua source code |
| `chunkname` | `string?` | Optional name for error messages |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function?` | The compiled function, or nil on error |
| `string?` | Error message if compilation failed |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

`loadstring` compiles Lua source code into a callable function. This is essential for dynamic code execution.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    local code = [[\
        local message = "Hello from loadstring!"\
        print(message)\
        return 42\
    ]]
    
    local func, err = loadstring(code)
    if func then
        local result = func()
        print("Returned:", result) -- 42
    else
        warn("Compile error:", err)
    end

[Loading from URL](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#loading-from-url)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local code = game:HttpGet("https://example.com/script.lua")
    local func, err = loadstring(code)
    if func then
        func()
    end

[With Error Handling](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#with-error-handling)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeLoadstring(code)
        local func, compileErr = loadstring(code)
        if not func then
            return nil, "Compile error: " .. tostring(compileErr)
        end
    
        local success, result = pcall(func)
        if not success then
            return nil, "Runtime error: " .. tostring(result)
        end
    
        return result
    end
    
    local result, err = safeLoadstring("return 1 + 1")
    if result then
        print("Result:", result)
    else
        warn(err)
    end

[Named Chunks](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#named-chunks)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Provide a name for better error messages
    local func = loadstring("error('test')", "MyScript")
    func() -- Error will reference "MyScript"

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------

*   Roblox normally disables `loadstring` for security
*   Volt re-enable this functionality
*   Always validate and sanitize code from external sources

[getsenv\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getsenv)
[Signals\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/signals)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring#description)

rconsoletoggle
==============

Toggles the console window visibility.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle#syntax)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    rconsoletoggle() -> void

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle#returns)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle#description)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`rconsoletoggle` toggles the visibility of the console window. If hidden, it shows the console; if visible, it hides the console.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle#example)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create console first
    rconsoleshow()
    rconsoleprint("Console is visible\n")
    
    -- Toggle it off
    rconsoletoggle()
    print("Console is now hidden")
    
    -- Toggle it back on
    rconsoletoggle()
    rconsoleprint("Console is visible again\n")

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoletoggle#related-functions)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`rconsoleshow`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsoleshow)
     - Show the console
*   [`rconsolehide`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehide)
     - Hide the console
*   [`rconsolehidden`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/console/rconsolehidden)
     - Check if hidden

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

makefolder
==========

Creates a new folder.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    makefolder(path: string) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The folder path to create |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`makefolder` creates a new folder at the specified path. Parent folders are created automatically if they don't exist.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a simple folder
    makefolder("configs")
    
    -- Create nested folders
    makefolder("data/saves/player1")
    
    -- Verify they exist
    print(isfolder("configs"))           -- true
    print(isfolder("data/saves/player1")) -- true

[Ensure Folder Exists](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#ensure-folder-exists)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function ensureFolder(path)
        if not isfolder(path) then
            makefolder(path)
            return true -- Created
        end
        return false -- Already existed
    end
    
    if ensureFolder("logs") then
        print("Created logs folder")
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`isfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/isfolder)
     - Check if folder exists
*   [`delfolder`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/delfolder)
     - Delete a folder
*   [`listfiles`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles)
     - List folder contents

# Volt Documentation

[Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts)

getscripthash
=============

Gets a hash of a script's bytecode.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    getscripthash(script: LocalScript | ModuleScript) -> string

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `script` | `LocalScript` or `ModuleScript` | The script |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `string` | A hash string of the bytecode |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#description)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getscripthash` returns a hash of a script's compiled bytecode. Scripts with identical code will have the same hash.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#example)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

    local scripts = getrunningscripts()
    if #scripts > 0 then
        local hash = getscripthash(scripts[1])
        print("Script hash:", hash)
    end

[Comparing Scripts](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#comparing-scripts)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function sameCode(script1, script2)
        return getscripthash(script1) == getscripthash(script2)
    end

[Tracking Changes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#tracking-changes)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local scriptHashes = {}
    
    local function hasScriptChanged(script)
        local currentHash = getscripthash(script)
        local previousHash = scriptHashes[script]
        
        scriptHashes[script] = currentHash
        
        return previousHash ~= nil and previousHash ~= currentHash
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#related-functions)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`getscriptbytecode`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptbytecode)
     - Get the actual bytecode
*   [`getfunctionhash`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/getfunctionhash)
     - Hash a function

[getscriptfromthread\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscriptfromthread)
[getscripts\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripts)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/getscripthash#example)

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

queueonteleport
===============

Queues a script to run after teleporting.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

    queueonteleport(script: string) -> void

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#aliases)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `queue_on_teleport`
*   `queueteleport`

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `script` | `string` | The Lua code to run after teleport |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`queueonteleport` queues Lua code to be executed after the player teleports to another place. The script will run once the new place loads.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Queue a script to run after teleporting
    queueonteleport([[\
        print("Teleported successfully!")\
        -- Your script code here\
    ]])
    
    -- Teleport the player
    game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(placeId)

[Auto-Execute Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#auto-execute-example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Queue the current script to run again
    queueonteleport(game:HttpGet("https://example.com/script.lua"))

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#notes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only one script can be queued at a time
*   Use `clearqueueonteleport` to clear the queue
*   The script runs in a fresh environment

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`clearqueueonteleport`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/clearqueueonteleport)
     - Clear the queue

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.getupvalues
=================

Gets all upvalues from a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.getupvalues(func: function | number) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | A table mapping indices to upvalue values |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.getupvalues` returns a table containing all upvalues (captured variables) of a function.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    local a = 1
    local b = "hello"
    local c = {key = "value"}
    
    local function example()
        print(a, b, c.key)
    end
    
    local upvalues = debug.getupvalues(example)
    for i, v in pairs(upvalues) do
        print(i, type(v), v)
    end
    --[[\
    Output:\
    1  number   1\
    2  string   hello\
    3  table    table: 0x...\
    ]]

[Practical Use](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#practical-use)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Find all string upvalues in a function
    local function getStringUpvalues(func)
        local strings = {}
        for i, upvalue in pairs(debug.getupvalues(func)) do
            if type(upvalue) == "string" then
                strings[i] = upvalue
            end
        end
        return strings
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue)
     - Get a single upvalue
*   [`debug.setupvalue`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue)
     - Modify an upvalue

[debug.getupvalue\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalue)
[debug.setconstant\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getupvalues#description)

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

request
=======

Makes an HTTP request.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#syntax)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    request(options: table) -> table

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#parameters)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `options` | `table` | Request configuration |

### [Options Table](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#options-table)

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Url` | `string` | The URL to request |
| `Method` | `string?` | HTTP method (GET, POST, etc.) |
| `Headers` | `table?` | Request headers |
| `Body` | `string?` | Request body |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#returns)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Response Table](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#response-table)

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Success` | `boolean` | Whether the request succeeded |
| `StatusCode` | `number` | HTTP status code |
| `StatusMessage` | `string` | HTTP status message |
| `Headers` | `table` | Response headers |
| `Body` | `string` | Response body |

[Example: GET Request](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#example-get-request)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local response = request({
        Url = "https://httpbin.org/get",
        Method = "GET"
    })
    
    if response.Success then
        print("Status:", response.StatusCode)
        print("Body:", response.Body)
    end

[Example: POST Request](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#example-post-request)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
    
    local response = request({
        Url = "https://httpbin.org/post",
        Method = "POST",
        Headers = {
            ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
        },
        Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
            username = "player",
            score = 100
        })
    })
    
    if response.Success then
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body)
        print(data)
    end

[Error Handling](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#error-handling)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local success, response = pcall(request, {
        Url = "https://example.com/api",
        Method = "GET"
    })
    
    if success and response.Success then
        print("Got data:", response.Body)
    elseif success then
        warn("HTTP Error:", response.StatusCode, response.StatusMessage)
    else
        warn("Request failed:", response)
    end

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#aliases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `http_request`
*   `http.request`

[queueonteleport\
\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/queueonteleport)
[saveinstance\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/request#returns)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.setstack
==============

Sets a value on the stack at a specific level and index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------

    debug.setstack(level: number, index: number, value: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `level` | `number` | The stack level (1 = current function) |
| `index` | `number` | The stack slot index |
| `value` | `any` | The new value to set |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.setstack` modifies a value on the call stack. This can change local variables in any active function on the stack.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#example)

------------------------------------------------------------

    local function modifier()
        debug.setstack(2, 1, "modified!")
    end
    
    local function example()
        local value = "original"
        modifier()
        print(value) -- "modified!"
    end
    
    example()

[Caution](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#caution)

------------------------------------------------------------

Modifying stack values can cause crashes or undefined behavior if:

*   You set an incompatible type
*   The index doesn't exist
*   The value is used in unexpected ways

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getstack`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getstack)
     - Get a stack value

Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setupvalue)

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

newcclosure
===========

Wraps a Luau function to appear as a C closure.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    newcclosure(func: function, debugname: string?) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The Luau function to wrap |
| `debugname` | `string?` | Optional name for debugging/stack traces |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A C closure wrapper that calls the original function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`newcclosure` wraps a Luau function so that it appears to be a C closure when inspected. The wrapped function behaves identically but `iscclosure` will return `true` for it.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function myHook(...)
        print("Hooked!")
        return ...
    end
    
    -- Check before wrapping
    print(iscclosure(myHook)) -- false
    
    -- Wrap it
    local wrapped = newcclosure(myHook)
    
    -- Now it appears as a C closure
    print(iscclosure(wrapped)) -- true
    
    -- But still works the same
    wrapped("test") -- Output: Hooked!

[With Debug Name](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#with-debug-name)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function handler()
        print("Handling request")
    end
    
    -- Wrap with a custom debug name
    local wrapped = newcclosure(handler, "RequestHandler")
    
    -- The debug name appears in stack traces and debug.info

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   The wrapper has minimal performance overhead
*   Errors are modified for hooking purposes
*   The optional `debugname` parameter sets the function name for debugging

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`newlclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure)
     - Wrap as Luau closure
*   [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
     - Check if C closure
*   [`isnewcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure)
     - Check if newcclosure

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/isnewcclosure)
[newlclosure\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure#description)

# Volt Documentation

[Filesystem](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem)

loadfile
========

Loads a Lua file and returns it as a function.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#syntax)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    loadfile(path: string) -> function?, string?

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#parameters)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `path` | `string` | The file path |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#returns)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function?` | The loaded function, or nil on error |
| `string?` | Error message if loading failed |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#description)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

`loadfile` reads a Lua file, compiles it, and returns it as a callable function. This is similar to `loadstring` but reads from a file.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#example)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a Lua file
    writefile("mymodule.lua", [[\
        local message = "Hello from file!"\
        return message\
    ]])
    
    -- Load and execute it
    local func, err = loadfile("mymodule.lua")
    if func then
        local result = func()
        print(result) -- "Hello from file!"
    else
        warn("Error:", err)
    end

[Module System](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#module-system)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Create a module file
    writefile("utils.lua", [[\
        local Utils = {}\
        \
        function Utils.greet(name)\
            return "Hello, " .. name .. "!"\
        end\
        \
        function Utils.add(a, b)\
            return a + b\
        end\
        \
        return Utils\
    ]])
    
    -- Load and use the module
    local Utils = loadfile("utils.lua")()
    print(Utils.greet("World")) -- "Hello, World!"
    print(Utils.add(2, 3))      -- 5

[Error Handling](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#error-handling)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    local function safeLoadFile(path)
        if not isfile(path) then
            return nil, "File not found"
        end
        return loadfile(path)
    end

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#related-functions)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`readfile`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/readfile)
     - Read raw file contents
*   [`loadstring`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/scripts/loadstring)
     - Load Lua from a string

\
Previous Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/listfiles)
[makefolder\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/makefolder)

### On this page

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#syntax)
[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#example)
[Module System](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/filesystem/loadfile#module-system)

# Volt Documentation

[Debug](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug)

debug.setconstant
=================

Sets a constant in a function at the specified index.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#syntax)

-------------------------------------------------------------

    debug.setconstant(func: function | number, index: number, value: any) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#parameters)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` or `number` | The function or stack level |
| `index` | `number` | The constant index (1-based) |
| `value` | `any` | The new value for the constant |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#returns)

---------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#description)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

`debug.setconstant` modifies a constant value in a function's bytecode. This allows you to change literal values that the function uses.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#example)

---------------------------------------------------------------

    local function greet()
        return "Hello, World!"
    end
    
    print(greet()) -- "Hello, World!"
    
    -- Find and change the string constant
    local constants = debug.getconstants(greet)
    for i, v in pairs(constants) do
        if v == "Hello, World!" then
            debug.setconstant(greet, i, "Goodbye, World!")
            break
        end
    end
    
    print(greet()) -- "Goodbye, World!"

[Caution](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#caution)

---------------------------------------------------------------

Modifying constants can cause unexpected behavior if:

*   The constant is used in multiple places
*   You set an incompatible type
*   The bytecode expects a specific value

[Use Cases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#use-cases)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Patching**: Change hardcoded values in game scripts
*   **Testing**: Modify behavior without changing source
*   **Bypasses**: Alter check values

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#related-functions)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`debug.getconstant`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstant)
     - Get a constant
*   [`debug.getconstants`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/getconstants)
     - Get all constants

\

[debug.setstack\
\
Next Page](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setstack)

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#parameters)
[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#returns)
[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#description)
[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/debug/setconstant#example)

getinstancecache
================

Gets all cached instance references.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstancecache#syntax)

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstancecache#returns)

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table` | Dictionary of cached instances |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/instances/getinstancecache#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`getinstancecache` returns a table containing all currently cached instance references.

    local cache = getinstancecache()

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

newlclosure
===========

Wraps a C closure to appear as a Luau closure.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------

    newlclosure(func: function) -> function

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The C closure to wrap |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `function` | A Luau closure wrapper that calls the original function |

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

`newlclosure` wraps a C closure so that it appears to be a Luau closure when inspected. The wrapped function behaves identically but `islclosure` will return `true` for it.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- print is a C closure
    print(iscclosure(print)) -- true
    print(islclosure(print)) -- false
    
    -- Wrap it as a Luau closure
    local wrappedPrint = newlclosure(print)
    
    -- Now it appears as a Luau closure
    print(iscclosure(wrappedPrint)) -- false
    print(islclosure(wrappedPrint)) -- true
    
    -- But still works the same
    wrappedPrint("Hello!") -- Output: Hello!

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------

*   The wrapper has minimal performance overhead

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newlclosure#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`newcclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/newcclosure)
     - Wrap as C closure
*   [`islclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/islclosure)
     - Check if Luau closure
*   [`iscclosure`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/iscclosure)
     - Check if C closure

# Volt Documentation

[Miscellaneous](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous)

saveinstance
============

Saves an instance (or the game) to a file.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#syntax)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    saveinstance(options: table?) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#parameters)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `options` | `table` | (Optional) Save options |

[Options](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#options)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Option | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `FilePath` | `string` | Output file path |
| `Object` | `Instance` | Instance to save (default: game) |
| `ExtraInstances` | `table` | Additional instances to include |
| `NilInstances` | `boolean` | Include nil-parented instances |
| `RemovePlayerCharacters` | `boolean` | Exclude player characters |
| `Mode` | `string` | "optimized", "full", or "scripts" |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#returns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#description)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`saveinstance` exports an instance hierarchy to an RBXL/RBXM file, which can be opened in Roblox Studio.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#example)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Save the entire game
    saveinstance({
        FilePath = "game.rbxl"
    })
    
    -- Save a specific model
    saveinstance({
        FilePath = "model.rbxm",
        Object = workspace.MyModel
    })
    
    -- Save with options
    saveinstance({
        FilePath = "full_game.rbxl",
        NilInstances = true,
        Mode = "full"
    })

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#notes)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

*   File is saved to the workspace folder
*   Large games may take time to save
*   Some instances may not save properly

[Related Functions](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveinstance#related-functions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`saveplace`](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/miscellaneous/saveplace)
     - Shorthand for saving game

# Volt Documentation

[Closures](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures)

restorefunction
===============

Restores a hooked function to its original implementation.

[Syntax](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#syntax)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

    restorefunction(func: function) -> void

[Parameters](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#parameters)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `func` | `function` | The hooked function to restore |

[Returns](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#returns)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

This function does not return a value.

[Description](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#description)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`restorefunction` removes a hook from a function, restoring it to its original behavior. This is useful for cleanup or when you need to temporarily remove a hook.

[Example](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#example)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- Hook print
    local originalPrint = hookfunction(print, function(...)
        originalPrint("[HOOKED]", ...)
    end)
    
    print("Test 1") -- Output: [HOOKED] Test 1
    
    -- Restore the original
    restorefunction(print)
    
    print("Test 2") -- Output: Test 2 (no prefix)

[Notes](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only works on functions that were hooked by volt
*   Has no effect on functions that aren't currently hooked
*   The original function reference from `hookfunction` remains valid

[Aliases](https://docs.volt.bz/docs/closures/restorefunction#aliases)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `restorefunc`
